import std.channel (Channel, Sender, Receiver)
import std.process (Process)
import std.string (String, StringBuffer)
import std.array (Array)
import std.hash (Hash, Hasher)
import std.map (Map)
import std.set (Set)
import std.option (Option, Some, None)
import std.result (Result, Ok, Err)
import std.iter (Iterator)
import std.io (Write, Read)
import std.fs (File, Path)
import std.time (Duration, Instant)
import std.sync (Mutex, RwLock)
import std.cmp (Ordering, Compare)
import std.fmt (Format, Formatter)

class TokenType {
    let @value: Int

    fn static word -> TokenType {
        TokenType { @value = 0 }
    }

    fn static punctuation -> TokenType {
        TokenType { @value = 1 }
    }

    fn static number -> TokenType {
        TokenType { @value = 2 }
    }

    fn static whitespace -> TokenType {
        TokenType { @value = 3 }
    }

    fn static special -> TokenType {
        TokenType { @value = 4 }
    }

    fn static subword -> TokenType {
        TokenType { @value = 5 }
    }

    fn static unknown -> TokenType {
        TokenType { @value = 6 }
    }

    fn static bos -> TokenType {
        TokenType { @value = 7 }
    }

    fn static eos -> TokenType {
        TokenType { @value = 8 }
    }

    fn static pad -> TokenType {
        TokenType { @value = 9 }
    }

    fn static mask -> TokenType {
        TokenType { @value = 10 }
    }
}

class Token {
    let @id: Int
    let @text: String
    let @token_type: TokenType
    let @start_pos: Int
    let @end_pos: Int
    let @attention_mask: Float
    let @position_id: Int
    let @segment_id: Int

    fn static new(id: Int, text: String, token_type: TokenType, start: Int, end: Int) -> Token {
        Token {
            @id = id,
            @text = text,
            @token_type = token_type,
            @start_pos = start,
            @end_pos = end,
            @attention_mask = 1.0,
            @position_id = 0,
            @segment_id = 0
        }
    }

    fn with_position(mut self, pos: Int) -> Token {
        @position_id = pos
        self
    }

    fn with_segment(mut self, seg: Int) -> Token {
        @segment_id = seg
        self
    }

    fn with_attention(mut self, att: Float) -> Token {
        @attention_mask = att
        self
    }
}

class VocabularyEntry {
    let @token: String
    let @id: Int
    let @frequency: Int
    let @score: Float
    let @is_special: Bool
    let @merge_priority: Int
}

class Vocabulary {
    let @token_to_id: Map[String, Int]
    let @id_to_token: Map[Int, String]
    let @frequencies: Map[Int, Int]
    let @scores: Map[Int, Float]
    let @special_tokens: Set[Int]
    let @size: Int
    let @unk_id: Int
    let @bos_id: Int
    let @eos_id: Int
    let @pad_id: Int
    let @mask_id: Int

    fn static new -> Vocabulary {
        let mut vocab = Vocabulary {
            @token_to_id = Map.new,
            @id_to_token = Map.new,
            @frequencies = Map.new,
            @scores = Map.new,
            @special_tokens = Set.new,
            @size = 0,
            @unk_id = 0,
            @bos_id = 1,
            @eos_id = 2,
            @pad_id = 3,
            @mask_id = 4
        }
        vocab.add_special_token("[UNK]", 0)
        vocab.add_special_token("[BOS]", 1)
        vocab.add_special_token("[EOS]", 2)
        vocab.add_special_token("[PAD]", 3)
        vocab.add_special_token("[MASK]", 4)
        vocab
    }

    fn mut add_special_token(token: String, id: Int) {
        @token_to_id.set(token, id)
        @id_to_token.set(id, token)
        @special_tokens.insert(id)
        @frequencies.set(id, 0)
        @scores.set(id, Float.infinity)
        if id >= @size {
            @size = id + 1
        }
    }

    fn mut add_token(token: String, frequency: Int, score: Float) -> Int {
        match @token_to_id.get(token) {
            case Some(id) -> {
                @frequencies.set(id, frequency)
                @scores.set(id, score)
                id
            }
            case None -> {
                let id = @size
                @token_to_id.set(token, id)
                @id_to_token.set(id, token)
                @frequencies.set(id, frequency)
                @scores.set(id, score)
                @size = @size + 1
                id
            }
        }
    }

    fn get_id(token: ref String) -> Option[Int] {
        @token_to_id.get(token)
    }

    fn get_token(id: Int) -> Option[String] {
        @id_to_token.get(id)
    }

    fn is_special(id: Int) -> Bool {
        @special_tokens.contains(id)
    }

    fn get_score(id: Int) -> Float {
        match @scores.get(id) {
            case Some(s) -> s
            case None -> 0.0
        }
    }
}

class BytePairEncoder {
    let @merges: Map[String, String]
    let @merge_ranks: Map[String, Int]
    let @cache: Map[String, Array[String]]
    let @max_cache_size: Int

    fn static new -> BytePairEncoder {
        BytePairEncoder {
            @merges = Map.new,
            @merge_ranks = Map.new,
            @cache = Map.new,
            @max_cache_size = 100000
        }
    }

    fn mut add_merge(pair: String, result: String, rank: Int) {
        @merges.set(pair, result)
        @merge_ranks.set(pair, rank)
    }

    fn get_pairs(word: ref Array[String]) -> Array[String] {
        let mut pairs = Array.new
        let len = word.size
        if len < 2 {
            return pairs
        }
        let mut i = 0
        loop {
            if i >= len - 1 {
                break
            }
            let pair = word.get(i).unwrap + " " + word.get(i + 1).unwrap
            pairs.push(pair)
            i = i + 1
        }
        pairs
    }

    fn mut encode(word: String) -> Array[String] {
        match @cache.get(word) {
            case Some(cached) -> return cached.clone
            case None -> {}
        }

        let mut chars = Array.new
        let mut iter = word.chars
        loop {
            match iter.next {
                case Some(c) -> chars.push(c.to_string)
                case None -> break
            }
        }

        if chars.size == 0 {
            return Array.new
        }

        if chars.size == 1 {
            return chars
        }

        loop {
            let pairs = get_pairs(chars)
            if pairs.size == 0 {
                break
            }

            let mut best_pair: Option[String] = None
            let mut best_rank = Int.max_value

            let mut idx = 0
            loop {
                if idx >= pairs.size {
                    break
                }
                let pair = pairs.get(idx).unwrap
                match @merge_ranks.get(pair) {
                    case Some(rank) -> {
                        if rank < best_rank {
                            best_rank = rank
                            best_pair = Some(pair)
                        }
                    }
                    case None -> {}
                }
                idx = idx + 1
            }

            match best_pair {
                case None -> break
                case Some(pair) -> {
                    let merged = @merges.get(pair).unwrap
                    let parts = pair.split(" ")
                    let first = parts.get(0).unwrap
                    let second = parts.get(1).unwrap
                    
                    let mut new_chars = Array.new
                    let mut i = 0
                    loop {
                        if i >= chars.size {
                            break
                        }
                        if i < chars.size - 1 {
                            let current = chars.get(i).unwrap
                            let next = chars.get(i + 1).unwrap
                            if current == first and next == second {
                                new_chars.push(merged)
                                i = i + 2
                            } else {
                                new_chars.push(current)
                                i = i + 1
                            }
                        } else {
                            new_chars.push(chars.get(i).unwrap)
                            i = i + 1
                        }
                    }
                    chars = new_chars
                }
            }
        }

        if @cache.size < @max_cache_size {
            @cache.set(word, chars.clone)
        }

        chars
    }
}

class WordPieceEncoder {
    let @vocab: ref Vocabulary
    let @max_word_length: Int
    let @unknown_token: String
    let @continuing_prefix: String

    fn static new(vocab: ref Vocabulary) -> WordPieceEncoder {
        WordPieceEncoder {
            @vocab = vocab,
            @max_word_length = 200,
            @unknown_token = "[UNK]",
            @continuing_prefix = "##"
        }
    }

    fn encode(word: String) -> Array[Int] {
        let mut tokens = Array.new
        
        if word.size > @max_word_length {
            tokens.push(@vocab.unk_id)
            return tokens
        }

        let mut start = 0
        let len = word.size

        loop {
            if start >= len {
                break
            }

            let mut end = len
            let mut found = false

            loop {
                if end <= start {
                    break
                }

                let mut substr = ""
                if start > 0 {
                    substr = @continuing_prefix + word.substring(start, end)
                } else {
                    substr = word.substring(start, end)
                }

                match @vocab.get_id(substr) {
                    case Some(id) -> {
                        tokens.push(id)
                        start = end
                        found = true
                        break
                    }
                    case None -> {
                        end = end - 1
                    }
                }
            }

            if found == false {
                tokens.push(@vocab.unk_id)
                start = start + 1
            }
        }

        tokens
    }
}

class UnigramEncoder {
    let @vocab: ref Vocabulary
    let @scores: Array[Float]
    let @min_score: Float

    fn static new(vocab: ref Vocabulary) -> UnigramEncoder {
        let mut scores = Array.new
        let mut i = 0
        loop {
            if i >= vocab.size {
                break
            }
            scores.push(vocab.get_score(i))
            i = i + 1
        }
        UnigramEncoder {
            @vocab = vocab,
            @scores = scores,
            @min_score = -Float.infinity
        }
    }

    fn viterbi_decode(text: String) -> Array[Int] {
        let len = text.size
        if len == 0 {
            return Array.new
        }

        let mut best_score = Array.with_capacity(len + 1)
        let mut best_edge = Array.with_capacity(len + 1)
        
        let mut i = 0
        loop {
            if i > len {
                break
            }
            best_score.push(@min_score)
            best_edge.push(-1)
            i = i + 1
        }
        best_score.set(0, 0.0)

        let mut end_pos = 1
        loop {
            if end_pos > len {
                break
            }

            let mut start_pos = 0
            loop {
                if start_pos >= end_pos {
                    break
                }

                let substr = text.substring(start_pos, end_pos)
                match @vocab.get_id(substr) {
                    case Some(id) -> {
                        let score = best_score.get(start_pos).unwrap + @scores.get(id).unwrap
                        if score > best_score.get(end_pos).unwrap {
                            best_score.set(end_pos, score)
                            best_edge.set(end_pos, start_pos)
                        }
                    }
                    case None -> {}
                }

                start_pos = start_pos + 1
            }

            end_pos = end_pos + 1
        }

        let mut tokens = Array.new
        let mut pos = len

        loop {
            if pos == 0 {
                break
            }

            let start = best_edge.get(pos).unwrap
            if start < 0 {
                tokens.push(@vocab.unk_id)
                pos = pos - 1
            } else {
                let substr = text.substring(start, pos)
                match @vocab.get_id(substr) {
                    case Some(id) -> tokens.push(id)
                    case None -> tokens.push(@vocab.unk_id)
                }
                pos = start
            }
        }

        tokens.reverse
        tokens
    }
}

class TokenizerMessage {
    let @message_type: Int
    let @text: String
    let @start_offset: Int
    let @end_offset: Int
    let @batch_id: Int
    let @sequence_id: Int
}

class TokenizerResult {
    let @tokens: Array[Token]
    let @batch_id: Int
    let @sequence_id: Int
    let @processing_time_ns: Int
    let @success: Bool
    let @error_message: String
}

class TokenizerWorker {
    let @worker_id: Int
    let @vocab: Vocabulary
    let @bpe: BytePairEncoder
    let @input: Receiver[TokenizerMessage]
    let @output: Sender[TokenizerResult]
    let @tokens_processed: Int
    let @errors_count: Int

    fn static spawn(
        worker_id: Int,
        vocab: Vocabulary,
        bpe: BytePairEncoder,
        input: Receiver[TokenizerMessage],
        output: Sender[TokenizerResult]
    ) -> Process {
        Process.spawn {
            let mut worker = TokenizerWorker {
                @worker_id = worker_id,
                @vocab = vocab,
                @bpe = bpe,
                @input = input,
                @output = output,
                @tokens_processed = 0,
                @errors_count = 0
            }
            worker.run
        }
    }

    fn mut run {
        loop {
            match @input.receive {
                case Some(message) -> {
                    if message.message_type == -1 {
                        break
                    }
                    let result = process_message(message)
                    @output.send(result)
                }
                case None -> break
            }
        }
    }

    fn mut process_message(message: TokenizerMessage) -> TokenizerResult {
        let start_time = Instant.now

        let text = message.text
        let mut tokens = Array.new

        if text.size == 0 {
            return TokenizerResult {
                @tokens = tokens,
                @batch_id = message.batch_id,
                @sequence_id = message.sequence_id,
                @processing_time_ns = 0,
                @success = true,
                @error_message = ""
            }
        }

        tokens.push(Token.new(@vocab.bos_id, "[BOS]", TokenType.bos, 0, 0))

        let words = split_into_words(text)
        let mut position = 1
        let mut char_offset = message.start_offset

        let mut word_idx = 0
        loop {
            if word_idx >= words.size {
                break
            }

            let word = words.get(word_idx).unwrap
            let word_len = word.size

            let subwords = @bpe.encode(word)
            
            let mut sub_idx = 0
            loop {
                if sub_idx >= subwords.size {
                    break
                }

                let subword = subwords.get(sub_idx).unwrap
                let subword_len = subword.size

                match @vocab.get_id(subword) {
                    case Some(id) -> {
                        let token = Token.new(
                            id,
                            subword,
                            TokenType.subword,
                            char_offset,
                            char_offset + subword_len
                        ).with_position(position)
                        tokens.push(token)
                        @tokens_processed = @tokens_processed + 1
                    }
                    case None -> {
                        let token = Token.new(
                            @vocab.unk_id,
                            subword,
                            TokenType.unknown,
                            char_offset,
                            char_offset + subword_len
                        ).with_position(position)
                        tokens.push(token)
                    }
                }

                char_offset = char_offset + subword_len
                position = position + 1
                sub_idx = sub_idx + 1
            }

            word_idx = word_idx + 1
        }

        tokens.push(Token.new(
            @vocab.eos_id,
            "[EOS]",
            TokenType.eos,
            char_offset,
            char_offset
        ).with_position(position))

        let elapsed = start_time.elapsed

        TokenizerResult {
            @tokens = tokens,
            @batch_id = message.batch_id,
            @sequence_id = message.sequence_id,
            @processing_time_ns = elapsed.as_nanos.to_int,
            @success = true,
            @error_message = ""
        }
    }

    fn split_into_words(text: String) -> Array[String] {
        let mut words = Array.new
        let mut current_word = StringBuffer.new
        let mut in_word = false

        let mut chars = text.chars
        loop {
            match chars.next {
                case Some(c) -> {
                    if is_whitespace(c) {
                        if in_word {
                            words.push(current_word.to_string)
                            current_word = StringBuffer.new
                            in_word = false
                        }
                    } else if is_punctuation(c) {
                        if in_word {
                            words.push(current_word.to_string)
                            current_word = StringBuffer.new
                            in_word = false
                        }
                        words.push(c.to_string)
                    } else {
                        current_word.push(c)
                        in_word = true
                    }
                }
                case None -> break
            }
        }

        if in_word {
            words.push(current_word.to_string)
        }

        words
    }

    fn is_whitespace(c: Char) -> Bool {
        c == ' ' or c == '\t' or c == '\n' or c == '\r'
    }

    fn is_punctuation(c: Char) -> Bool {
        let code = c.to_int
        (code >= 33 and code <= 47) or
        (code >= 58 and code <= 64) or
        (code >= 91 and code <= 96) or
        (code >= 123 and code <= 126)
    }
}

class ParallelTokenizer {
    let @vocab: Vocabulary
    let @bpe: BytePairEncoder
    let @num_workers: Int
    let @input_channels: Array[Sender[TokenizerMessage]]
    let @output_channel: Receiver[TokenizerResult]
    let @output_sender: Sender[TokenizerResult]
    let @workers: Array[Process]
    let @batch_counter: Int
    let @pending_results: Map[Int, Array[TokenizerResult]]
    let @max_sequence_length: Int
    let @pad_to_max_length: Bool

    fn static new(vocab: Vocabulary, num_workers: Int) -> ParallelTokenizer {
        let (output_sender, output_receiver) = Channel.new

        let mut input_channels = Array.new
        let mut workers = Array.new
        let bpe = BytePairEncoder.new

        let mut i = 0
        loop {
            if i >= num_workers {
                break
            }

            let (input_sender, input_receiver) = Channel.new
            input_channels.push(input_sender)

            let worker = TokenizerWorker.spawn(
                i,
                vocab.clone,
                bpe.clone,
                input_receiver,
                output_sender.clone
            )
            workers.push(worker)

            i = i + 1
        }

        ParallelTokenizer {
            @vocab = vocab,
            @bpe = bpe,
            @num_workers = num_workers,
            @input_channels = input_channels,
            @output_channel = output_receiver,
            @output_sender = output_sender,
            @workers = workers,
            @batch_counter = 0,
            @pending_results = Map.new,
            @max_sequence_length = 512,
            @pad_to_max_length = true
        }
    }

    fn mut tokenize_batch(texts: Array[String]) -> Array[Array[Token]] {
        let batch_id = @batch_counter
        @batch_counter = @batch_counter + 1

        let num_texts = texts.size
        if num_texts == 0 {
            return Array.new
        }

        let mut idx = 0
        loop {
            if idx >= num_texts {
                break
            }

            let text = texts.get(idx).unwrap
            let worker_idx = idx % @num_workers
            let message = TokenizerMessage {
                @message_type = 0,
                @text = text,
                @start_offset = 0,
                @end_offset = text.size,
                @batch_id = batch_id,
                @sequence_id = idx
            }

            @input_channels.get(worker_idx).unwrap.send(message)
            idx = idx + 1
        }

        let mut results = Array.with_capacity(num_texts)
        let mut i = 0
        loop {
            if i >= num_texts {
                break
            }
            results.push(Array.new)
            i = i + 1
        }

        let mut received = 0
        loop {
            if received >= num_texts {
                break
            }

            match @output_channel.receive {
                case Some(result) -> {
                    if result.batch_id == batch_id {
                        results.set(result.sequence_id, result.tokens)
                        received = received + 1
                    }
                }
                case None -> break
            }
        }

        if @pad_to_max_length {
            results = pad_sequences(results)
        }

        results
    }

    fn mut tokenize_single(text: String) -> Array[Token] {
        let batch = Array.with_element(text)
        let results = tokenize_batch(batch)
        match results.get(0) {
            case Some(tokens) -> tokens
            case None -> Array.new
        }
    }

    fn pad_sequences(sequences: Array[Array[Token]]) -> Array[Array[Token]] {
        let mut max_len = 0
        let mut idx = 0
        loop {
            if idx >= sequences.size {
                break
            }
            let seq = sequences.get(idx).unwrap
            if seq.size > max_len {
                max_len = seq.size
            }
            idx = idx + 1
        }

        if max_len > @max_sequence_length {
            max_len = @max_sequence_length
        }

        let mut padded = Array.new
        idx = 0
        loop {
            if idx >= sequences.size {
                break
            }

            let seq = sequences.get(idx).unwrap
            let mut new_seq = Array.new

            let mut token_idx = 0
            loop {
                if token_idx >= max_len {
                    break
                }

                if token_idx < seq.size {
                    new_seq.push(seq.get(token_idx).unwrap)
                } else {
                    let pad_token = Token.new(
                        @vocab.pad_id,
                        "[PAD]",
                        TokenType.pad,
                        0,
                        0
                    ).with_position(token_idx).with_attention(0.0)
                    new_seq.push(pad_token)
                }

                token_idx = token_idx + 1
            }

            padded.push(new_seq)
            idx = idx + 1
        }

        padded
    }

    fn decode(token_ids: Array[Int]) -> String {
        let mut result = StringBuffer.new
        let mut idx = 0

        loop {
            if idx >= token_ids.size {
                break
            }

            let id = token_ids.get(idx).unwrap
            if @vocab.is_special(id) == false {
                match @vocab.get_token(id) {
                    case Some(token) -> {
                        let cleaned = token.replace("##", "")
                        result.push_string(cleaned)
                    }
                    case None -> {}
                }
            }

            idx = idx + 1
        }

        result.to_string
    }

    fn mut shutdown {
        let mut i = 0
        loop {
            if i >= @num_workers {
                break
            }

            let message = TokenizerMessage {
                @message_type = -1,
                @text = "",
                @start_offset = 0,
                @end_offset = 0,
                @batch_id = -1,
                @sequence_id = -1
            }
            @input_channels.get(i).unwrap.send(message)
            i = i + 1
        }
    }
}

class PreTokenizer {
    let @split_on_whitespace: Bool
    let @split_on_punctuation: Bool
    let @lowercase: Bool
    let @strip_accents: Bool
    let @handle_chinese_chars: Bool
    let @nfd_normalize: Bool

    fn static default -> PreTokenizer {
        PreTokenizer {
            @split_on_whitespace = true,
            @split_on_punctuation = true,
            @lowercase = true,
            @strip_accents = true,
            @handle_chinese_chars = true,
            @nfd_normalize = true
        }
    }

    fn process(text: String) -> Array[String] {
        let mut current = text

        if @lowercase {
            current = current.to_lowercase
        }

        if @strip_accents {
            current = remove_accents(current)
        }

        if @handle_chinese_chars {
            current = add_chinese_whitespace(current)
        }

        let mut tokens = Array.new
        let mut current_token = StringBuffer.new

        let mut chars = current.chars
        loop {
            match chars.next {
                case Some(c) -> {
                    if @split_on_whitespace and is_whitespace(c) {
                        if current_token.size > 0 {
                            tokens.push(current_token.to_string)
                            current_token = StringBuffer.new
                        }
                    } else if @split_on_punctuation and is_punctuation_char(c) {
                        if current_token.size > 0 {
                            tokens.push(current_token.to_string)
                            current_token = StringBuffer.new
                        }
                        tokens.push(c.to_string)
                    } else {
                        current_token.push(c)
                    }
                }
                case None -> break
            }
        }

        if current_token.size > 0 {
            tokens.push(current_token.to_string)
        }

        tokens
    }

    fn is_whitespace(c: Char) -> Bool {
        c == ' ' or c == '\t' or c == '\n' or c == '\r'
    }

    fn is_punctuation_char(c: Char) -> Bool {
        let code = c.to_int
        (code >= 33 and code <= 47) or
        (code >= 58 and code <= 64) or
        (code >= 91 and code <= 96) or
        (code >= 123 and code <= 126)
    }

    fn remove_accents(text: String) -> String {
        text
    }

    fn add_chinese_whitespace(text: String) -> String {
        let mut result = StringBuffer.new
        let mut chars = text.chars
        loop {
            match chars.next {
                case Some(c) -> {
                    if is_chinese_char(c) {
                        result.push(' ')
                        result.push(c)
                        result.push(' ')
                    } else {
                        result.push(c)
                    }
                }
                case None -> break
            }
        }
        result.to_string
    }

    fn is_chinese_char(c: Char) -> Bool {
        let cp = c.to_int
        (cp >= 0x4E00 and cp <= 0x9FFF) or
        (cp >= 0x3400 and cp <= 0x4DBF) or
        (cp >= 0x20000 and cp <= 0x2A6DF) or
        (cp >= 0x2A700 and cp <= 0x2B73F) or
        (cp >= 0x2B740 and cp <= 0x2B81F) or
        (cp >= 0x2B820 and cp <= 0x2CEAF) or
        (cp >= 0xF900 and cp <= 0xFAFF) or
        (cp >= 0x2F800 and cp <= 0x2FA1F)
    }
}

class PostProcessor {
    let @add_special_tokens: Bool
    let @bos_token_id: Int
    let @eos_token_id: Int
    let @sep_token_id: Int
    let @cls_token_id: Int

    fn static default(vocab: ref Vocabulary) -> PostProcessor {
        PostProcessor {
            @add_special_tokens = true,
            @bos_token_id = vocab.bos_id,
            @eos_token_id = vocab.eos_id,
            @sep_token_id = vocab.eos_id,
            @cls_token_id = vocab.bos_id
        }
    }

    fn process_single(tokens: Array[Int]) -> Array[Int] {
        if @add_special_tokens == false {
            return tokens
        }

        let mut result = Array.with_capacity(tokens.size + 2)
        result.push(@cls_token_id)

        let mut i = 0
        loop {
            if i >= tokens.size {
                break
            }
            result.push(tokens.get(i).unwrap)
            i = i + 1
        }

        result.push(@sep_token_id)
        result
    }

    fn process_pair(tokens_a: Array[Int], tokens_b: Array[Int]) -> Array[Int] {
        if @add_special_tokens == false {
            let mut result = tokens_a.clone
            let mut i = 0
            loop {
                if i >= tokens_b.size {
                    break
                }
                result.push(tokens_b.get(i).unwrap)
                i = i + 1
            }
            return result
        }

        let mut result = Array.with_capacity(tokens_a.size + tokens_b.size + 3)
        result.push(@cls_token_id)

        let mut i = 0
        loop {
            if i >= tokens_a.size {
                break
            }
            result.push(tokens_a.get(i).unwrap)
            i = i + 1
        }

        result.push(@sep_token_id)

        i = 0
        loop {
            if i >= tokens_b.size {
                break
            }
            result.push(tokens_b.get(i).unwrap)
            i = i + 1
        }

        result.push(@sep_token_id)
        result
    }

    fn get_segment_ids(tokens_a_len: Int, tokens_b_len: Int) -> Array[Int] {
        let mut segments = Array.new
        
        let total_a = tokens_a_len + 2
        let mut i = 0
        loop {
            if i >= total_a {
                break
            }
            segments.push(0)
            i = i + 1
        }

        let total_b = tokens_b_len + 1
        i = 0
        loop {
            if i >= total_b {
                break
            }
            segments.push(1)
            i = i + 1
        }

        segments
    }
}

class TokenizerConfig {
    let @vocab_size: Int
    let @max_sequence_length: Int
    let @pad_token: String
    let @unk_token: String
    let @bos_token: String
    let @eos_token: String
    let @mask_token: String
    let @do_lowercase: Bool
    let @do_strip_accents: Bool
    let @num_workers: Int
    let @batch_size: Int

    fn static default -> TokenizerConfig {
        TokenizerConfig {
            @vocab_size = 32000,
            @max_sequence_length = 512,
            @pad_token = "[PAD]",
            @unk_token = "[UNK]",
            @bos_token = "[BOS]",
            @eos_token = "[EOS]",
            @mask_token = "[MASK]",
            @do_lowercase = true,
            @do_strip_accents = true,
            @num_workers = 4,
            @batch_size = 32
        }
    }
}

class Tokenizer {
    let @config: TokenizerConfig
    let @vocab: Vocabulary
    let @pre_tokenizer: PreTokenizer
    let @post_processor: PostProcessor
    let @parallel: ParallelTokenizer

    fn static new(config: TokenizerConfig) -> Tokenizer {
        let vocab = Vocabulary.new
        let pre_tokenizer = PreTokenizer.default
        let post_processor = PostProcessor.default(vocab)
        let parallel = ParallelTokenizer.new(vocab.clone, config.num_workers)

        Tokenizer {
            @config = config,
            @vocab = vocab,
            @pre_tokenizer = pre_tokenizer,
            @post_processor = post_processor,
            @parallel = parallel
        }
    }

    fn mut encode(text: String) -> Array[Int] {
        let tokens = @parallel.tokenize_single(text)
        let mut ids = Array.new

        let mut i = 0
        loop {
            if i >= tokens.size {
                break
            }
            ids.push(tokens.get(i).unwrap.id)
            i = i + 1
        }

        ids
    }

    fn mut encode_batch(texts: Array[String]) -> Array[Array[Int]] {
        let token_arrays = @parallel.tokenize_batch(texts)
        let mut id_arrays = Array.new

        let mut batch_idx = 0
        loop {
            if batch_idx >= token_arrays.size {
                break
            }

            let tokens = token_arrays.get(batch_idx).unwrap
            let mut ids = Array.new

            let mut token_idx = 0
            loop {
                if token_idx >= tokens.size {
                    break
                }
                ids.push(tokens.get(token_idx).unwrap.id)
                token_idx = token_idx + 1
            }

            id_arrays.push(ids)
            batch_idx = batch_idx + 1
        }

        id_arrays
    }

    fn decode(ids: Array[Int]) -> String {
        @parallel.decode(ids)
    }

    fn vocab_size -> Int {
        @vocab.size
    }

    fn mut shutdown {
        @parallel.shutdown
    }
}

class pub Main {
    fn pub static main {
        let config = TokenizerConfig.default
        let mut tokenizer = Tokenizer.new(config)

        let texts = [
            "Hello world, this is a test.",
            "Natural language processing is fascinating.",
            "Parallel tokenization improves performance."
        ]

        let mut array = Array.new
        let mut i = 0
        loop {
            if i >= 3 {
                break
            }
            array.push(texts.get(i).unwrap)
            i = i + 1
        }

        let results = tokenizer.encode_batch(array)

        tokenizer.shutdown
    }
}

File: ./optimizer/optimizer_core.lobster
import std
import vec
import color

enum OptimizerType:
    sgd_optimizer
    momentum_optimizer
    nesterov_optimizer
    adagrad_optimizer
    rmsprop_optimizer
    adam_optimizer
    adamw_optimizer
    lamb_optimizer
    lars_optimizer
    radam_optimizer
    nadam_optimizer
    adafactor_optimizer

class OptimizerConfig:
    learning_rate: float
    weight_decay: float
    momentum: float
    beta1: float
    beta2: float
    epsilon: float
    dampening: float
    nesterov: bool
    amsgrad: bool
    maximize: bool
    foreach_enabled: bool
    fused: bool
    capturable: bool
    differentiable: bool

    def default() -> OptimizerConfig:
        OptimizerConfig {
            learning_rate: 0.001,
            weight_decay: 0.0,
            momentum: 0.0,
            beta1: 0.9,
            beta2: 0.999,
            epsilon: 1e-8,
            dampening: 0.0,
            nesterov: false,
            amsgrad: false,
            maximize: false,
            foreach_enabled: true,
            fused: false,
            capturable: false,
            differentiable: false
        }

    def with_learning_rate(lr: float) -> OptimizerConfig:
        learning_rate = lr
        return this

    def with_weight_decay(wd: float) -> OptimizerConfig:
        weight_decay = wd
        return this

    def with_momentum(m: float) -> OptimizerConfig:
        momentum = m
        return this

    def with_betas(b1: float, b2: float) -> OptimizerConfig:
        beta1 = b1
        beta2 = b2
        return this

class ParameterState:
    step: int
    exp_avg: [float]
    exp_avg_sq: [float]
    max_exp_avg_sq: [float]
    momentum_buffer: [float]
    sum_grad: [float]
    grad_avg: [float]
    grad_sq_sum: [float]

    def new(size: int) -> ParameterState:
        let zeros: [float] = []
        for i in size:
            push(zeros, 0.0)
        ParameterState {
            step: 0,
            exp_avg: copy(zeros),
            exp_avg_sq: copy(zeros),
            max_exp_avg_sq: copy(zeros),
            momentum_buffer: copy(zeros),
            sum_grad: copy(zeros),
            grad_avg: copy(zeros),
            grad_sq_sum: copy(zeros)
        }

    def reset():
        step = 0
        for i in length(exp_avg):
            exp_avg[i] = 0.0
            exp_avg_sq[i] = 0.0
            max_exp_avg_sq[i] = 0.0
            momentum_buffer[i] = 0.0

class ParameterGroup:
    params: [[float]]
    grads: [[float]]
    states: [ParameterState]
    config: OptimizerConfig
    group_id: int

    def new(group_id: int, config: OptimizerConfig) -> ParameterGroup:
        ParameterGroup {
            params: [],
            grads: [],
            states: [],
            config: config,
            group_id: group_id
        }

    def add_parameter(param: [float], grad: [float]):
        push(params, param)
        push(grads, grad)
        push(states, ParameterState.new(length(param)))

    def num_parameters() -> int:
        return length(params)

    def total_elements() -> int:
        var total = 0
        for p in params:
            total += length(p)
        return total

class BaseOptimizer:
    param_groups: [ParameterGroup]
    defaults: OptimizerConfig
    global_step: int
    optimizer_type: OptimizerType

    def new(config: OptimizerConfig, opt_type: OptimizerType) -> BaseOptimizer:
        BaseOptimizer {
            param_groups: [],
            defaults: config,
            global_step: 0,
            optimizer_type: opt_type
        }

    def add_param_group(group: ParameterGroup):
        push(param_groups, group)

    def zero_grad():
        for group in param_groups:
            for grad in group.grads:
                for i in length(grad):
                    grad[i] = 0.0

    def step():
        global_step += 1

    def state_dict() -> [[float]]:
        let states: [[float]] = []
        for group in param_groups:
            for state in group.states:
                push(states, copy(state.exp_avg))
        return states

    def load_state_dict(states: [[float]]):
        var idx = 0
        for group in param_groups:
            for state in group.states:
                if idx < length(states):
                    state.exp_avg = copy(states[idx])
                    idx += 1

class SGDOptimizer:
    base: BaseOptimizer

    def new(config: OptimizerConfig) -> SGDOptimizer:
        SGDOptimizer {
            base: BaseOptimizer.new(config, sgd_optimizer)
        }

    def step():
        base.step()
        
        for group in base.param_groups:
            let lr = group.config.learning_rate
            let wd = group.config.weight_decay
            let momentum = group.config.momentum
            let dampening = group.config.dampening
            let nesterov = group.config.nesterov
            
            for p_idx in length(group.params):
                let param = group.params[p_idx]
                let grad = group.grads[p_idx]
                var state = group.states[p_idx]
                
                for i in length(param):
                    var d_p = grad[i]
                    
                    if wd != 0.0:
                        d_p += wd * param[i]
                    
                    if momentum != 0.0:
                        if state.step == 0:
                            state.momentum_buffer[i] = d_p
                        else:
                            state.momentum_buffer[i] = momentum * state.momentum_buffer[i] + (1.0 - dampening) * d_p
                        
                        if nesterov:
                            d_p = d_p + momentum * state.momentum_buffer[i]
                        else:
                            d_p = state.momentum_buffer[i]
                    
                    param[i] -= lr * d_p
                
                state.step += 1

    def zero_grad():
        base.zero_grad()

class AdamOptimizer:
    base: BaseOptimizer

    def new(config: OptimizerConfig) -> AdamOptimizer:
        AdamOptimizer {
            base: BaseOptimizer.new(config, adam_optimizer)
        }

    def step():
        base.step()
        
        for group in base.param_groups:
            let lr = group.config.learning_rate
            let beta1 = group.config.beta1
            let beta2 = group.config.beta2
            let eps = group.config.epsilon
            let wd = group.config.weight_decay
            let amsgrad = group.config.amsgrad
            
            for p_idx in length(group.params):
                let param = group.params[p_idx]
                let grad = group.grads[p_idx]
                var state = group.states[p_idx]
                
                state.step += 1
                
                let bias_correction1 = 1.0 - pow(beta1, float(state.step))
                let bias_correction2 = 1.0 - pow(beta2, float(state.step))
                
                for i in length(param):
                    var g = grad[i]
                    
                    if wd != 0.0:
                        g += wd * param[i]
                    
                    state.exp_avg[i] = beta1 * state.exp_avg[i] + (1.0 - beta1) * g
                    state.exp_avg_sq[i] = beta2 * state.exp_avg_sq[i] + (1.0 - beta2) * g * g
                    
                    var denom: float
                    if amsgrad:
                        state.max_exp_avg_sq[i] = max(state.max_exp_avg_sq[i], state.exp_avg_sq[i])
                        denom = sqrt(state.max_exp_avg_sq[i] / bias_correction2) + eps
                    else:
                        denom = sqrt(state.exp_avg_sq[i] / bias_correction2) + eps
                    
                    let step_size = lr / bias_correction1
                    param[i] -= step_size * state.exp_avg[i] / denom

    def zero_grad():
        base.zero_grad()

class AdamWOptimizer:
    base: BaseOptimizer

    def new(config: OptimizerConfig) -> AdamWOptimizer:
        AdamWOptimizer {
            base: BaseOptimizer.new(config, adamw_optimizer)
        }

    def step():
        base.step()
        
        for group in base.param_groups:
            let lr = group.config.learning_rate
            let beta1 = group.config.beta1
            let beta2 = group.config.beta2
            let eps = group.config.epsilon
            let wd = group.config.weight_decay
            let amsgrad = group.config.amsgrad
            
            for p_idx in length(group.params):
                let param = group.params[p_idx]
                let grad = group.grads[p_idx]
                var state = group.states[p_idx]
                
                state.step += 1
                
                for i in length(param):
                    param[i] -= lr * wd * param[i]
                
                let bias_correction1 = 1.0 - pow(beta1, float(state.step))
                let bias_correction2 = 1.0 - pow(beta2, float(state.step))
                
                for i in length(param):
                    let g = grad[i]
                    
                    state.exp_avg[i] = beta1 * state.exp_avg[i] + (1.0 - beta1) * g
                    state.exp_avg_sq[i] = beta2 * state.exp_avg_sq[i] + (1.0 - beta2) * g * g
                    
                    var denom: float
                    if amsgrad:
                        state.max_exp_avg_sq[i] = max(state.max_exp_avg_sq[i], state.exp_avg_sq[i])
                        denom = sqrt(state.max_exp_avg_sq[i] / bias_correction2) + eps
                    else:
                        denom = sqrt(state.exp_avg_sq[i] / bias_correction2) + eps
                    
                    let step_size = lr / bias_correction1
                    param[i] -= step_size * state.exp_avg[i] / denom

    def zero_grad():
        base.zero_grad()

class RMSpropOptimizer:
    base: BaseOptimizer
    alpha: float
    centered: bool

    def new(config: OptimizerConfig) -> RMSpropOptimizer:
        RMSpropOptimizer {
            base: BaseOptimizer.new(config, rmsprop_optimizer),
            alpha: 0.99,
            centered: false
        }

    def step():
        base.step()
        
        for group in base.param_groups:
            let lr = group.config.learning_rate
            let eps = group.config.epsilon
            let wd = group.config.weight_decay
            let momentum = group.config.momentum
            
            for p_idx in length(group.params):
                let param = group.params[p_idx]
                let grad = group.grads[p_idx]
                var state = group.states[p_idx]
                
                state.step += 1
                
                for i in length(param):
                    var g = grad[i]
                    
                    if wd != 0.0:
                        g += wd * param[i]
                    
                    state.exp_avg_sq[i] = alpha * state.exp_avg_sq[i] + (1.0 - alpha) * g * g
                    
                    var avg: float
                    if centered:
                        state.grad_avg[i] = alpha * state.grad_avg[i] + (1.0 - alpha) * g
                        avg = state.exp_avg_sq[i] - state.grad_avg[i] * state.grad_avg[i]
                    else:
                        avg = state.exp_avg_sq[i]
                    
                    if momentum > 0.0:
                        state.momentum_buffer[i] = momentum * state.momentum_buffer[i] + g / (sqrt(avg) + eps)
                        param[i] -= lr * state.momentum_buffer[i]
                    else:
                        param[i] -= lr * g / (sqrt(avg) + eps)

    def zero_grad():
        base.zero_grad()

class AdagradOptimizer:
    base: BaseOptimizer
    lr_decay: float
    initial_accumulator_value: float

    def new(config: OptimizerConfig) -> AdagradOptimizer:
        AdagradOptimizer {
            base: BaseOptimizer.new(config, adagrad_optimizer),
            lr_decay: 0.0,
            initial_accumulator_value: 0.0
        }

    def step():
        base.step()
        
        for group in base.param_groups:
            let lr = group.config.learning_rate
            let eps = group.config.epsilon
            let wd = group.config.weight_decay
            
            for p_idx in length(group.params):
                let param = group.params[p_idx]
                let grad = group.grads[p_idx]
                var state = group.states[p_idx]
                
                if state.step == 0:
                    for i in length(param):
                        state.sum_grad[i] = initial_accumulator_value
                
                state.step += 1
                
                let adjusted_lr = lr / (1.0 + float(state.step - 1) * lr_decay)
                
                for i in length(param):
                    var g = grad[i]
                    
                    if wd != 0.0:
                        g += wd * param[i]
                    
                    state.sum_grad[i] += g * g
                    param[i] -= adjusted_lr * g / (sqrt(state.sum_grad[i]) + eps)

    def zero_grad():
        base.zero_grad()

class LAMBOptimizer:
    base: BaseOptimizer
    trust_clip: bool

    def new(config: OptimizerConfig) -> LAMBOptimizer:
        LAMBOptimizer {
            base: BaseOptimizer.new(config, lamb_optimizer),
            trust_clip: true
        }

    def step():
        base.step()
        
        for group in base.param_groups:
            let lr = group.config.learning_rate
            let beta1 = group.config.beta1
            let beta2 = group.config.beta2
            let eps = group.config.epsilon
            let wd = group.config.weight_decay
            
            for p_idx in length(group.params):
                let param = group.params[p_idx]
                let grad = group.grads[p_idx]
                var state = group.states[p_idx]
                
                state.step += 1
                
                let bias_correction1 = 1.0 - pow(beta1, float(state.step))
                let bias_correction2 = 1.0 - pow(beta2, float(state.step))
                
                var weight_norm = 0.0
                for i in length(param):
                    weight_norm += param[i] * param[i]
                weight_norm = sqrt(weight_norm)
                
                var adam_step: [float] = []
                var adam_norm = 0.0
                
                for i in length(param):
                    let g = grad[i]
                    
                    state.exp_avg[i] = beta1 * state.exp_avg[i] + (1.0 - beta1) * g
                    state.exp_avg_sq[i] = beta2 * state.exp_avg_sq[i] + (1.0 - beta2) * g * g
                    
                    let m_hat = state.exp_avg[i] / bias_correction1
                    let v_hat = state.exp_avg_sq[i] / bias_correction2
                    
                    var step_val = m_hat / (sqrt(v_hat) + eps)
                    if wd > 0.0:
                        step_val += wd * param[i]
                    
                    push(adam_step, step_val)
                    adam_norm += step_val * step_val
                
                adam_norm = sqrt(adam_norm)
                
                var trust_ratio = 1.0
                if weight_norm > 0.0 and adam_norm > 0.0:
                    trust_ratio = weight_norm / adam_norm
                    if trust_clip:
                        trust_ratio = min(trust_ratio, 10.0)
                
                for i in length(param):
                    param[i] -= lr * trust_ratio * adam_step[i]

    def zero_grad():
        base.zero_grad()

class LARSOptimizer:
    base: BaseOptimizer
    trust_coefficient: float
    trust_clip: bool
    eps: float

    def new(config: OptimizerConfig) -> LARSOptimizer:
        LARSOptimizer {
            base: BaseOptimizer.new(config, lars_optimizer),
            trust_coefficient: 0.001,
            trust_clip: true,
            eps: 1e-8
        }

    def step():
        base.step()
        
        for group in base.param_groups:
            let lr = group.config.learning_rate
            let wd = group.config.weight_decay
            let momentum = group.config.momentum
            let dampening = group.config.dampening
            
            for p_idx in length(group.params):
                let param = group.params[p_idx]
                let grad = group.grads[p_idx]
                var state = group.states[p_idx]
                
                state.step += 1
                
                var weight_norm = 0.0
                var grad_norm = 0.0
                for i in length(param):
                    weight_norm += param[i] * param[i]
                    grad_norm += grad[i] * grad[i]
                weight_norm = sqrt(weight_norm)
                grad_norm = sqrt(grad_norm)
                
                var local_lr = 1.0
                if weight_norm > eps and grad_norm > eps:
                    local_lr = trust_coefficient * weight_norm / (grad_norm + wd * weight_norm + eps)
                    if trust_clip:
                        local_lr = min(local_lr, 1.0)
                
                for i in length(param):
                    var d_p = grad[i]
                    
                    if wd != 0.0:
                        d_p += wd * param[i]
                    
                    d_p *= local_lr
                    
                    if momentum != 0.0:
                        if state.step == 1:
                            state.momentum_buffer[i] = d_p
                        else:
                            state.momentum_buffer[i] = momentum * state.momentum_buffer[i] + (1.0 - dampening) * d_p
                        d_p = state.momentum_buffer[i]
                    
                    param[i] -= lr * d_p

    def zero_grad():
        base.zero_grad()

class RAdamOptimizer:
    base: BaseOptimizer
    rho_inf: float

    def new(config: OptimizerConfig) -> RAdamOptimizer:
        RAdamOptimizer {
            base: BaseOptimizer.new(config, radam_optimizer),
            rho_inf: 0.0
        }

    def compute_rho_inf(beta2: float) -> float:
        return 2.0 / (1.0 - beta2) - 1.0

    def step():
        base.step()
        
        for group in base.param_groups:
            let lr = group.config.learning_rate
            let beta1 = group.config.beta1
            let beta2 = group.config.beta2
            let eps = group.config.epsilon
            let wd = group.config.weight_decay
            
            let rho_inf_val = compute_rho_inf(beta2)
            
            for p_idx in length(group.params):
                let param = group.params[p_idx]
                let grad = group.grads[p_idx]
                var state = group.states[p_idx]
                
                state.step += 1
                
                let bias_correction1 = 1.0 - pow(beta1, float(state.step))
                let bias_correction2 = 1.0 - pow(beta2, float(state.step))
                
                let beta2_t = pow(beta2, float(state.step))
                let rho_t = rho_inf_val - 2.0 * float(state.step) * beta2_t / bias_correction2
                
                for i in length(param):
                    var g = grad[i]
                    
                    if wd != 0.0:
                        g += wd * param[i]
                    
                    state.exp_avg[i] = beta1 * state.exp_avg[i] + (1.0 - beta1) * g
                    state.exp_avg_sq[i] = beta2 * state.exp_avg_sq[i] + (1.0 - beta2) * g * g
                    
                    let m_hat = state.exp_avg[i] / bias_correction1
                    
                    if rho_t > 5.0:
                        let v_hat = state.exp_avg_sq[i] / bias_correction2
                        let rect = sqrt((rho_t - 4.0) * (rho_t - 2.0) * rho_inf_val / ((rho_inf_val - 4.0) * (rho_inf_val - 2.0) * rho_t))
                        param[i] -= lr * rect * m_hat / (sqrt(v_hat) + eps)
                    else:
                        param[i] -= lr * m_hat

    def zero_grad():
        base.zero_grad()

class NAdamOptimizer:
    base: BaseOptimizer

    def new(config: OptimizerConfig) -> NAdamOptimizer:
        NAdamOptimizer {
            base: BaseOptimizer.new(config, nadam_optimizer)
        }

    def step():
        base.step()
        
        for group in base.param_groups:
            let lr = group.config.learning_rate
            let beta1 = group.config.beta1
            let beta2 = group.config.beta2
            let eps = group.config.epsilon
            let wd = group.config.weight_decay
            
            for p_idx in length(group.params):
                let param = group.params[p_idx]
                let grad = group.grads[p_idx]
                var state = group.states[p_idx]
                
                state.step += 1
                
                let bias_correction1 = 1.0 - pow(beta1, float(state.step))
                let bias_correction2 = 1.0 - pow(beta2, float(state.step))
                let bias_correction1_next = 1.0 - pow(beta1, float(state.step + 1))
                
                for i in length(param):
                    var g = grad[i]
                    
                    if wd != 0.0:
                        param[i] -= lr * wd * param[i]
                    
                    state.exp_avg[i] = beta1 * state.exp_avg[i] + (1.0 - beta1) * g
                    state.exp_avg_sq[i] = beta2 * state.exp_avg_sq[i] + (1.0 - beta2) * g * g
                    
                    let m_hat = state.exp_avg[i] / bias_correction1
                    let m_hat_next = state.exp_avg[i] / bias_correction1_next
                    let v_hat = state.exp_avg_sq[i] / bias_correction2
                    
                    let m_nadam = (1.0 - beta1) * g / bias_correction1 + beta1 * m_hat_next
                    
                    param[i] -= lr * m_nadam / (sqrt(v_hat) + eps)

    def zero_grad():
        base.zero_grad()

class AdafactorOptimizer:
    base: BaseOptimizer
    scale_parameter: bool
    relative_step: bool
    warmup_init: bool
    clip_threshold: float
    decay_rate: float
    beta1: float
    rms_eps: float

    def new(config: OptimizerConfig) -> AdafactorOptimizer:
        AdafactorOptimizer {
            base: BaseOptimizer.new(config, adafactor_optimizer),
            scale_parameter: true,
            relative_step: true,
            warmup_init: false,
            clip_threshold: 1.0,
            decay_rate: -0.8,
            beta1: 0.0,
            rms_eps: 1e-30
        }

    def compute_rms(tensor: [float]) -> float:
        var sum_sq = 0.0
        for v in tensor:
            sum_sq += v * v
        return sqrt(sum_sq / float(length(tensor)))

    def get_lr(base_lr: float, step: int) -> float:
        if relative_step:
            var min_step = 1e-6
            if warmup_init:
                min_step = 1e-2 * float(step)
            return min(base_lr, 1.0 / sqrt(float(step)))
        return base_lr

    def get_rho(step: int) -> float:
        return min(0.3, 1.0 / pow(float(step), 1.0 - decay_rate))

    def step():
        base.step()
        
        for group in base.param_groups:
            let base_lr = group.config.learning_rate
            
            for p_idx in length(group.params):
                let param = group.params[p_idx]
                let grad = group.grads[p_idx]
                var state = group.states[p_idx]
                
                state.step += 1
                
                let lr = get_lr(base_lr, state.step)
                let rho = get_rho(state.step)
                
                var alpha = lr
                if scale_parameter:
                    let rms = compute_rms(param)
                    alpha = lr * max(1e-3, rms)
                
                for i in length(param):
                    let g = grad[i]
                    
                    state.exp_avg_sq[i] = rho * state.exp_avg_sq[i] + (1.0 - rho) * g * g
                    
                    let v_hat = state.exp_avg_sq[i]
                    let update_scale = 1.0 / (sqrt(v_hat) + rms_eps)
                    
                    var update = g * update_scale
                    
                    let rms_update = compute_rms([update])
                    if rms_update > clip_threshold:
                        update = update * clip_threshold / rms_update
                    
                    if beta1 > 0.0:
                        state.exp_avg[i] = beta1 * state.exp_avg[i] + (1.0 - beta1) * update
                        update = state.exp_avg[i]
                    
                    param[i] -= alpha * update

    def zero_grad():
        base.zero_grad()

class LRScheduler:
    base_lr: float
    current_lr: float
    step_count: int
    last_epoch: int

    def new(base_lr: float) -> LRScheduler:
        LRScheduler {
            base_lr: base_lr,
            current_lr: base_lr,
            step_count: 0,
            last_epoch: -1
        }

    def get_lr() -> float:
        return current_lr

    def step():
        step_count += 1
        last_epoch += 1

class StepLR:
    scheduler: LRScheduler
    step_size: int
    gamma: float

    def new(base_lr: float, step_size: int, gamma: float) -> StepLR:
        StepLR {
            scheduler: LRScheduler.new(base_lr),
            step_size: step_size,
            gamma: gamma
        }

    def step():
        scheduler.step()
        let epoch = scheduler.last_epoch
        let num_decays = epoch / step_size
        scheduler.current_lr = scheduler.base_lr * pow(gamma, float(num_decays))

    def get_lr() -> float:
        return scheduler.get_lr()

class ExponentialLR:
    scheduler: LRScheduler
    gamma: float

    def new(base_lr: float, gamma: float) -> ExponentialLR:
        ExponentialLR {
            scheduler: LRScheduler.new(base_lr),
            gamma: gamma
        }

    def step():
        scheduler.step()
        scheduler.current_lr = scheduler.base_lr * pow(gamma, float(scheduler.last_epoch))

    def get_lr() -> float:
        return scheduler.get_lr()

class CosineAnnealingLR:
    scheduler: LRScheduler
    t_max: int
    eta_min: float

    def new(base_lr: float, t_max: int, eta_min: float) -> CosineAnnealingLR:
        CosineAnnealingLR {
            scheduler: LRScheduler.new(base_lr),
            t_max: t_max,
            eta_min: eta_min
        }

    def step():
        scheduler.step()
        let epoch = scheduler.last_epoch
        let cos_inner = 3.14159265359 * float(epoch) / float(t_max)
        scheduler.current_lr = eta_min + (scheduler.base_lr - eta_min) * (1.0 + cos(cos_inner)) / 2.0

    def get_lr() -> float:
        return scheduler.get_lr()

class WarmupLR:
    scheduler: LRScheduler
    warmup_steps: int
    target_lr: float

    def new(target_lr: float, warmup_steps: int) -> WarmupLR:
        WarmupLR {
            scheduler: LRScheduler.new(0.0),
            warmup_steps: warmup_steps,
            target_lr: target_lr
        }

    def step():
        scheduler.step()
        let step = scheduler.step_count
        if step <= warmup_steps:
            scheduler.current_lr = target_lr * float(step) / float(warmup_steps)
        else:
            scheduler.current_lr = target_lr

    def get_lr() -> float:
        return scheduler.get_lr()

class WarmupCosineAnnealingLR:
    scheduler: LRScheduler
    warmup_steps: int
    total_steps: int
    eta_min: float

    def new(base_lr: float, warmup_steps: int, total_steps: int, eta_min: float) -> WarmupCosineAnnealingLR:
        WarmupCosineAnnealingLR {
            scheduler: LRScheduler.new(base_lr),
            warmup_steps: warmup_steps,
            total_steps: total_steps,
            eta_min: eta_min
        }

    def step():
        scheduler.step()
        let step = scheduler.step_count
        
        if step <= warmup_steps:
            scheduler.current_lr = scheduler.base_lr * float(step) / float(warmup_steps)
        else:
            let progress = float(step - warmup_steps) / float(total_steps - warmup_steps)
            let cos_inner = 3.14159265359 * progress
            scheduler.current_lr = eta_min + (scheduler.base_lr - eta_min) * (1.0 + cos(cos_inner)) / 2.0

    def get_lr() -> float:
        return scheduler.get_lr()

class PolynomialLR:
    scheduler: LRScheduler
    total_iters: int
    power: float
    end_lr: float

    def new(base_lr: float, total_iters: int, power: float, end_lr: float) -> PolynomialLR:
        PolynomialLR {
            scheduler: LRScheduler.new(base_lr),
            total_iters: total_iters,
            power: power,
            end_lr: end_lr
        }

    def step():
        scheduler.step()
        let step = min(scheduler.step_count, total_iters)
        let decay = pow(1.0 - float(step) / float(total_iters), power)
        scheduler.current_lr = (scheduler.base_lr - end_lr) * decay + end_lr

    def get_lr() -> float:
        return scheduler.get_lr()

class OneCycleLR:
    scheduler: LRScheduler
    max_lr: float
    total_steps: int
    pct_start: float
    div_factor: float
    final_div_factor: float
    anneal_strategy: string

    def new(max_lr: float, total_steps: int) -> OneCycleLR:
        OneCycleLR {
            scheduler: LRScheduler.new(max_lr / 25.0),
            max_lr: max_lr,
            total_steps: total_steps,
            pct_start: 0.3,
            div_factor: 25.0,
            final_div_factor: 10000.0,
            anneal_strategy: "cos"
        }

    def step():
        scheduler.step()
        let step = scheduler.step_count
        let initial_lr = max_lr / div_factor
        let final_lr = initial_lr / final_div_factor
        
        let step1 = int(float(total_steps) * pct_start)
        let step2 = total_steps - step1
        
        if step <= step1:
            let pct = float(step) / float(step1)
            scheduler.current_lr = initial_lr + (max_lr - initial_lr) * pct
        else:
            let pct = float(step - step1) / float(step2)
            if anneal_strategy == "cos":
                let cos_inner = 3.14159265359 * pct
                scheduler.current_lr = final_lr + (max_lr - final_lr) * (1.0 + cos(cos_inner)) / 2.0
            else:
                scheduler.current_lr = max_lr - (max_lr - final_lr) * pct

    def get_lr() -> float:
        return scheduler.get_lr()

class ReduceLROnPlateau:
    scheduler: LRScheduler
    mode: string
    factor: float
    patience: int
    threshold: float
    threshold_mode: string
    cooldown: int
    min_lr: float
    best: float
    num_bad_epochs: int
    cooldown_counter: int

    def new(base_lr: float, mode: string, factor: float, patience: int) -> ReduceLROnPlateau:
        let initial_best = if mode == "min": 1e38 else: -1e38
        ReduceLROnPlateau {
            scheduler: LRScheduler.new(base_lr),
            mode: mode,
            factor: factor,
            patience: patience,
            threshold: 1e-4,
            threshold_mode: "rel",
            cooldown: 0,
            min_lr: 0.0,
            best: initial_best,
            num_bad_epochs: 0,
            cooldown_counter: 0
        }

    def is_better(current: float) -> bool:
        if mode == "min":
            if threshold_mode == "rel":
                return current < best * (1.0 - threshold)
            else:
                return current < best - threshold
        else:
            if threshold_mode == "rel":
                return current > best * (1.0 + threshold)
            else:
                return current > best + threshold

    def step_with_metric(metric: float):
        scheduler.step()
        
        if cooldown_counter > 0:
            cooldown_counter -= 1
            num_bad_epochs = 0
            return
        
        if is_better(metric):
            best = metric
            num_bad_epochs = 0
        else:
            num_bad_epochs += 1
        
        if num_bad_epochs > patience:
            scheduler.current_lr = max(scheduler.current_lr * factor, min_lr)
            cooldown_counter = cooldown
            num_bad_epochs = 0

    def get_lr() -> float:
        return scheduler.get_lr()

def create_optimizer(opt_type: OptimizerType, config: OptimizerConfig):
    switch opt_type:
        case sgd_optimizer:
            return SGDOptimizer.new(config)
        case adam_optimizer:
            return AdamOptimizer.new(config)
        case adamw_optimizer:
            return AdamWOptimizer.new(config)
        case rmsprop_optimizer:
            return RMSpropOptimizer.new(config)
        case adagrad_optimizer:
            return AdagradOptimizer.new(config)
        case lamb_optimizer:
            return LAMBOptimizer.new(config)
        case lars_optimizer:
            return LARSOptimizer.new(config)
        case radam_optimizer:
            return RAdamOptimizer.new(config)
        case nadam_optimizer:
            return NAdamOptimizer.new(config)
        case adafactor_optimizer:
            return AdafactorOptimizer.new(config)
        default:
            return AdamOptimizer.new(config)

def run_optimizer_test():
    let config = OptimizerConfig.default()
    let optimizer = AdamOptimizer.new(config)
    
    let params = [1.0, 2.0, 3.0, 4.0]
    let grads = [0.1, 0.2, 0.3, 0.4]
    
    var group = ParameterGroup.new(0, config)
    group.add_parameter(params, grads)
    optimizer.base.add_param_group(group)
    
    for i in 100:
        optimizer.step()
    
    print("Optimizer test completed")
    print("Final params: " + string(params))

def main():
    run_optimizer_test()
