inline float fast_exp(float x) {
    float t = 1.0f + x / 256.0f;
    t = t * t; t = t * t; t = t * t; t = t * t;
    t = t * t; t = t * t; t = t * t; t = t * t;
    return t;
}

inline float fast_tanh(float x) {
    float x2 = x * x;
    float a = x * (135135.0f + x2 * (17325.0f + x2 * (378.0f + x2)));
    float b = 135135.0f + x2 * (62370.0f + x2 * (3150.0f + x2 * 28.0f));
    return a / b;
}

inline float fast_sigmoid(float x) {
    return 1.0f / (1.0f + fast_exp(-x));
}

inline float fast_gelu(float x) {
    float x3 = x * x * x;
    float inner = 0.797884560803f * (x + 0.044715f * x3);
    return 0.5f * x * (1.0f + fast_tanh(inner));
}

inline float fast_silu(float x) {
    return x * fast_sigmoid(x);
}

inline float fast_rsqrt(float x) {
    float xhalf = 0.5f * x;
    int i = floatbits(x);
    i = 0x5f375a86 - (i >> 1);
    float y = intbits(i);
    y = y * (1.5f - xhalf * y * y);
    y = y * (1.5f - xhalf * y * y);
    return y;
}

export void vector_add(
    uniform float output[],
    uniform float input_a[],
    uniform float input_b[],
    uniform int size
) {
    foreach (i = 0 ... size) {
        output[i] = input_a[i] + input_b[i];
    }
}

export void vector_subtract(
    uniform float output[],
    uniform float input_a[],
    uniform float input_b[],
    uniform int size
) {
    foreach (i = 0 ... size) {
        output[i] = input_a[i] - input_b[i];
    }
}

export void vector_multiply(
    uniform float output[],
    uniform float input_a[],
    uniform float input_b[],
    uniform int size
) {
    foreach (i = 0 ... size) {
        output[i] = input_a[i] * input_b[i];
    }
}

export void vector_divide(
    uniform float output[],
    uniform float input_a[],
    uniform float input_b[],
    uniform int size
) {
    foreach (i = 0 ... size) {
        float b = input_b[i];
        if (abs(b) > 1e-10f) {
            output[i] = input_a[i] / b;
        } else {
            output[i] = 0.0f;
        }
    }
}

export void vector_scale(
    uniform float output[],
    uniform float input[],
    uniform float scale,
    uniform int size
) {
    foreach (i = 0 ... size) {
        output[i] = input[i] * scale;
    }
}

export void vector_add_scalar(
    uniform float output[],
    uniform float input[],
    uniform float scalar,
    uniform int size
) {
    foreach (i = 0 ... size) {
        output[i] = input[i] + scalar;
    }
}

export void vector_fma(
    uniform float output[],
    uniform float input_a[],
    uniform float input_b[],
    uniform float input_c[],
    uniform int size
) {
    foreach (i = 0 ... size) {
        output[i] = input_a[i] * input_b[i] + input_c[i];
    }
}

export void vector_relu(
    uniform float output[],
    uniform float input[],
    uniform int size
) {
    foreach (i = 0 ... size) {
        output[i] = max(0.0f, input[i]);
    }
}

export void vector_leaky_relu(
    uniform float output[],
    uniform float input[],
    uniform float alpha,
    uniform int size
) {
    foreach (i = 0 ... size) {
        float x = input[i];
        output[i] = x > 0.0f ? x : alpha * x;
    }
}

export void vector_elu(
    uniform float output[],
    uniform float input[],
    uniform float alpha,
    uniform int size
) {
    foreach (i = 0 ... size) {
        float x = input[i];
        output[i] = x > 0.0f ? x : alpha * (fast_exp(x) - 1.0f);
    }
}

export void vector_sigmoid(
    uniform float output[],
    uniform float input[],
    uniform int size
) {
    foreach (i = 0 ... size) {
        output[i] = fast_sigmoid(input[i]);
    }
}

export void vector_tanh(
    uniform float output[],
    uniform float input[],
    uniform int size
) {
    foreach (i = 0 ... size) {
        output[i] = fast_tanh(input[i]);
    }
}

export void vector_gelu(
    uniform float output[],
    uniform float input[],
    uniform int size
) {
    foreach (i = 0 ... size) {
        output[i] = fast_gelu(input[i]);
    }
}

export void vector_silu(
    uniform float output[],
    uniform float input[],
    uniform int size
) {
    foreach (i = 0 ... size) {
        output[i] = fast_silu(input[i]);
    }
}

export void vector_softplus(
    uniform float output[],
    uniform float input[],
    uniform float beta,
    uniform float threshold,
    uniform int size
) {
    foreach (i = 0 ... size) {
        float x = input[i];
        float bx = beta * x;
        if (bx > threshold) {
            output[i] = x;
        } else {
            output[i] = log(1.0f + fast_exp(bx)) / beta;
        }
    }
}

export void matmul_blocked(
    uniform float C[],
    uniform float A[],
    uniform float B[],
    uniform int M,
    uniform int N,
    uniform int K,
    uniform int lda,
    uniform int ldb,
    uniform int ldc
) {
    uniform int BLOCK_M = 64;
    uniform int BLOCK_N = 64;
    uniform int BLOCK_K = 64;

    for (uniform int i0 = 0; i0 < M; i0 += BLOCK_M) {
        for (uniform int j0 = 0; j0 < N; j0 += BLOCK_N) {
            uniform int i_end = min(i0 + BLOCK_M, M);
            uniform int j_end = min(j0 + BLOCK_N, N);

            for (uniform int k0 = 0; k0 < K; k0 += BLOCK_K) {
                uniform int k_end = min(k0 + BLOCK_K, K);

                for (uniform int i = i0; i < i_end; i++) {
                    foreach (j = j0 ... j_end) {
                        float sum = 0.0f;
                        for (uniform int k = k0; k < k_end; k++) {
                            sum += A[i * lda + k] * B[k * ldb + j];
                        }
                        if (k0 == 0) {
                            C[i * ldc + j] = sum;
                        } else {
                            C[i * ldc + j] += sum;
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

export void matmul_transposed_b(
    uniform float C[],
    uniform float A[],
    uniform float B[],
    uniform int M,
    uniform int N,
    uniform int K,
    uniform int lda,
    uniform int ldb,
    uniform int ldc
) {
    uniform int BLOCK = 32;

    for (uniform int i0 = 0; i0 < M; i0 += BLOCK) {
        for (uniform int j0 = 0; j0 < N; j0 += BLOCK) {
            uniform int i_end = min(i0 + BLOCK, M);
            uniform int j_end = min(j0 + BLOCK, N);

            for (uniform int i = i0; i < i_end; i++) {
                foreach (j = j0 ... j_end) {
                    float sum = 0.0f;
                    for (uniform int k = 0; k < K; k++) {
                        sum += A[i * lda + k] * B[j * ldb + k];
                    }
                    C[i * ldc + j] = sum;
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

export void batch_matmul(
    uniform float C[],
    uniform float A[],
    uniform float B[],
    uniform int batch_size,
    uniform int M,
    uniform int N,
    uniform int K
) {
    uniform int A_batch_stride = M * K;
    uniform int B_batch_stride = K * N;
    uniform int C_batch_stride = M * N;

    for (uniform int b = 0; b < batch_size; b++) {
        uniform float * uniform A_ptr = A + b * A_batch_stride;
        uniform float * uniform B_ptr = B + b * B_batch_stride;
        uniform float * uniform C_ptr = C + b * C_batch_stride;

        for (uniform int i = 0; i < M; i++) {
            foreach (j = 0 ... N) {
                float sum = 0.0f;
                for (uniform int k = 0; k < K; k++) {
                    sum += A_ptr[i * K + k] * B_ptr[k * N + j];
                }
                C_ptr[i * N + j] = sum;
            }
        }
    }
}

export void softmax_forward(
    uniform float output[],
    uniform float input[],
    uniform int batch_size,
    uniform int dim
) {
    for (uniform int b = 0; b < batch_size; b++) {
        uniform int offset = b * dim;

        float max_val = input[offset];
        for (uniform int i = 1; i < dim; i++) {
            max_val = max(max_val, input[offset + i]);
        }
        uniform float max_reduced = reduce_max(max_val);

        float sum_exp = 0.0f;
        foreach (i = 0 ... dim) {
            float exp_val = fast_exp(input[offset + i] - max_reduced);
            output[offset + i] = exp_val;
            sum_exp += exp_val;
        }
        uniform float sum_reduced = reduce_add(sum_exp);

        float inv_sum = 1.0f / sum_reduced;
        foreach (i = 0 ... dim) {
            output[offset + i] = output[offset + i] * inv_sum;
        }
    }
}

export void layer_norm_forward(
    uniform float output[],
    uniform float input[],
    uniform float gamma[],
    uniform float beta[],
    uniform float mean_out[],
    uniform float var_out[],
    uniform int batch_size,
    uniform int hidden_size,
    uniform float epsilon
) {
    for (uniform int b = 0; b < batch_size; b++) {
        uniform int offset = b * hidden_size;

        float sum = 0.0f;
        foreach (i = 0 ... hidden_size) {
            sum += input[offset + i];
        }
        uniform float mean = reduce_add(sum) / hidden_size;
        mean_out[b] = mean;

        float var_sum = 0.0f;
        foreach (i = 0 ... hidden_size) {
            float diff = input[offset + i] - mean;
            var_sum += diff * diff;
        }
        uniform float variance = reduce_add(var_sum) / hidden_size;
        var_out[b] = variance;

        uniform float inv_std = fast_rsqrt(variance + epsilon);

        foreach (i = 0 ... hidden_size) {
            float normalized = (input[offset + i] - mean) * inv_std;
            output[offset + i] = normalized * gamma[i] + beta[i];
        }
    }
}

export void rms_norm_forward(
    uniform float output[],
    uniform float input[],
    uniform float weight[],
    uniform int batch_size,
    uniform int hidden_size,
    uniform float epsilon
) {
    for (uniform int b = 0; b < batch_size; b++) {
        uniform int offset = b * hidden_size;

        float sum_sq = 0.0f;
        foreach (i = 0 ... hidden_size) {
            float x = input[offset + i];
            sum_sq += x * x;
        }
        uniform float mean_sq = reduce_add(sum_sq) / hidden_size;
        uniform float rms = fast_rsqrt(mean_sq + epsilon);

        foreach (i = 0 ... hidden_size) {
            output[offset + i] = input[offset + i] * rms * weight[i];
        }
    }
}

export void attention_scores(
    uniform float scores[],
    uniform float queries[],
    uniform float keys[],
    uniform int batch_size,
    uniform int num_heads,
    uniform int seq_length,
    uniform int head_dim,
    uniform float scale
) {
    uniform int head_stride = seq_length * head_dim;
    uniform int batch_stride = num_heads * head_stride;
    uniform int score_head_stride = seq_length * seq_length;
    uniform int score_batch_stride = num_heads * score_head_stride;

    for (uniform int b = 0; b < batch_size; b++) {
        for (uniform int h = 0; h < num_heads; h++) {
            uniform float * uniform Q = queries + b * batch_stride + h * head_stride;
            uniform float * uniform K = keys + b * batch_stride + h * head_stride;
            uniform float * uniform S = scores + b * score_batch_stride + h * score_head_stride;

            for (uniform int i = 0; i < seq_length; i++) {
                foreach (j = 0 ... seq_length) {
                    float dot = 0.0f;
                    for (uniform int d = 0; d < head_dim; d++) {
                        dot += Q[i * head_dim + d] * K[j * head_dim + d];
                    }
                    S[i * seq_length + j] = dot * scale;
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

export void attention_output(
    uniform float output[],
    uniform float attention_weights[],
    uniform float values[],
    uniform int batch_size,
    uniform int num_heads,
    uniform int seq_length,
    uniform int head_dim
) {
    uniform int head_stride = seq_length * head_dim;
    uniform int batch_stride = num_heads * head_stride;
    uniform int attn_head_stride = seq_length * seq_length;
    uniform int attn_batch_stride = num_heads * attn_head_stride;

    for (uniform int b = 0; b < batch_size; b++) {
        for (uniform int h = 0; h < num_heads; h++) {
            uniform float * uniform A = attention_weights + b * attn_batch_stride + h * attn_head_stride;
            uniform float * uniform V = values + b * batch_stride + h * head_stride;
            uniform float * uniform O = output + b * batch_stride + h * head_stride;

            for (uniform int i = 0; i < seq_length; i++) {
                foreach (d = 0 ... head_dim) {
                    float sum = 0.0f;
                    for (uniform int j = 0; j < seq_length; j++) {
                        sum += A[i * seq_length + j] * V[j * head_dim + d];
                    }
                    O[i * head_dim + d] = sum;
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

export void causal_mask(
    uniform float scores[],
    uniform int batch_size,
    uniform int num_heads,
    uniform int seq_length
) {
    uniform int head_stride = seq_length * seq_length;
    uniform int batch_stride = num_heads * head_stride;
    uniform float neg_inf = -1e9f;

    for (uniform int b = 0; b < batch_size; b++) {
        for (uniform int h = 0; h < num_heads; h++) {
            uniform float * uniform S = scores + b * batch_stride + h * head_stride;

            for (uniform int i = 0; i < seq_length; i++) {
                foreach (j = 0 ... seq_length) {
                    if (j > i) {
                        S[i * seq_length + j] = neg_inf;
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

export void conv2d_forward(
    uniform float output[],
    uniform float input[],
    uniform float weights[],
    uniform float bias[],
    uniform ConvolutionParams params
) {
    uniform int B = params.batch_size;
    uniform int IC = params.in_channels;
    uniform int OC = params.out_channels;
    uniform int IH = params.in_height;
    uniform int IW = params.in_width;
    uniform int OH = params.out_height;
    uniform int OW = params.out_width;
    uniform int KH = params.kernel_height;
    uniform int KW = params.kernel_width;
    uniform int SH = params.stride_h;
    uniform int SW = params.stride_w;
    uniform int PH = params.pad_h;
    uniform int PW = params.pad_w;
    uniform int DH = params.dilation_h;
    uniform int DW = params.dilation_w;
    uniform int G = params.groups;

    uniform int IC_per_group = IC / G;
    uniform int OC_per_group = OC / G;

    for (uniform int b = 0; b < B; b++) {
        for (uniform int g = 0; g < G; g++) {
            for (uniform int oc = 0; oc < OC_per_group; oc++) {
                uniform int oc_abs = g * OC_per_group + oc;

                for (uniform int oh = 0; oh < OH; oh++) {
                    foreach (ow = 0 ... OW) {
                        float sum = bias != NULL ? bias[oc_abs] : 0.0f;

                        for (uniform int ic = 0; ic < IC_per_group; ic++) {
                            uniform int ic_abs = g * IC_per_group + ic;

                            for (uniform int kh = 0; kh < KH; kh++) {
                                for (uniform int kw = 0; kw < KW; kw++) {
                                    int ih = oh * SH - PH + kh * DH;
                                    int iw = ow * SW - PW + kw * DW;

                                    if (ih >= 0 && ih < IH && iw >= 0 && iw < IW) {
                                        int input_idx = ((b * IC + ic_abs) * IH + ih) * IW + iw;
                                        int weight_idx = ((oc_abs * IC_per_group + ic) * KH + kh) * KW + kw;
                                        sum += input[input_idx] * weights[weight_idx];
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        }

                        int output_idx = ((b * OC + oc_abs) * OH + oh) * OW + ow;
                        output[output_idx] = sum;
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

export void max_pool2d_forward(
    uniform float output[],
    uniform int indices[],
    uniform float input[],
    uniform PoolingParams params
) {
    uniform int B = params.batch_size;
    uniform int C = params.channels;
    uniform int IH = params.in_height;
    uniform int IW = params.in_width;
    uniform int OH = params.out_height;
    uniform int OW = params.out_width;
    uniform int KH = params.kernel_height;
    uniform int KW = params.kernel_width;
    uniform int SH = params.stride_h;
    uniform int SW = params.stride_w;
    uniform int PH = params.pad_h;
    uniform int PW = params.pad_w;

    for (uniform int b = 0; b < B; b++) {
        for (uniform int c = 0; c < C; c++) {
            for (uniform int oh = 0; oh < OH; oh++) {
                foreach (ow = 0 ... OW) {
                    float max_val = -1e38f;
                    int max_idx = -1;

                    for (uniform int kh = 0; kh < KH; kh++) {
                        for (uniform int kw = 0; kw < KW; kw++) {
                            int ih = oh * SH - PH + kh;
                            int iw = ow * SW - PW + kw;

                            if (ih >= 0 && ih < IH && iw >= 0 && iw < IW) {
                                int input_idx = ((b * C + c) * IH + ih) * IW + iw;
                                float val = input[input_idx];
                                if (val > max_val) {
                                    max_val = val;
                                    max_idx = input_idx;
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }

                    int output_idx = ((b * C + c) * OH + oh) * OW + ow;
                    output[output_idx] = max_val;
                    if (indices != NULL) {
                        indices[output_idx] = max_idx;
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

export void avg_pool2d_forward(
    uniform float output[],
    uniform float input[],
    uniform PoolingParams params
) {
    uniform int B = params.batch_size;
    uniform int C = params.channels;
    uniform int IH = params.in_height;
    uniform int IW = params.in_width;
    uniform int OH = params.out_height;
    uniform int OW = params.out_width;
    uniform int KH = params.kernel_height;
    uniform int KW = params.kernel_width;
    uniform int SH = params.stride_h;
    uniform int SW = params.stride_w;
    uniform int PH = params.pad_h;
    uniform int PW = params.pad_w;

    for (uniform int b = 0; b < B; b++) {
        for (uniform int c = 0; c < C; c++) {
            for (uniform int oh = 0; oh < OH; oh++) {
                foreach (ow = 0 ... OW) {
                    float sum = 0.0f;
                    int count = 0;

                    for (uniform int kh = 0; kh < KH; kh++) {
                        for (uniform int kw = 0; kw < KW; kw++) {
                            int ih = oh * SH - PH + kh;
                            int iw = ow * SW - PW + kw;

                            if (ih >= 0 && ih < IH && iw >= 0 && iw < IW) {
                                int input_idx = ((b * C + c) * IH + ih) * IW + iw;
                                sum += input[input_idx];
                                count += 1;
                            }
                        }
                    }

                    int output_idx = ((b * C + c) * OH + oh) * OW + ow;
                    output[output_idx] = count > 0 ? sum / count : 0.0f;
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

export void batch_norm_forward(
    uniform float output[],
    uniform float input[],
    uniform float gamma[],
    uniform float beta[],
    uniform float running_mean[],
    uniform float running_var[],
    uniform float batch_mean[],
    uniform float batch_var[],
    uniform BatchNormParams params
) {
    uniform int B = params.batch_size;
    uniform int C = params.channels;
    uniform int S = params.spatial_size;
    uniform float eps = params.epsilon;
    uniform float momentum = params.momentum;
    uniform int training = params.training;

    if (training) {
        for (uniform int c = 0; c < C; c++) {
            float sum = 0.0f;
            for (uniform int b = 0; b < B; b++) {
                foreach (s = 0 ... S) {
                    sum += input[(b * C + c) * S + s];
                }
            }
            uniform float mean = reduce_add(sum) / (B * S);
            batch_mean[c] = mean;

            float var_sum = 0.0f;
            for (uniform int b = 0; b < B; b++) {
                foreach (s = 0 ... S) {
                    float diff = input[(b * C + c) * S + s] - mean;
                    var_sum += diff * diff;
                }
            }
            uniform float var = reduce_add(var_sum) / (B * S);
            batch_var[c] = var;

            running_mean[c] = (1.0f - momentum) * running_mean[c] + momentum * mean;
            running_var[c] = (1.0f - momentum) * running_var[c] + momentum * var;

            uniform float inv_std = fast_rsqrt(var + eps);

            for (uniform int b = 0; b < B; b++) {
                foreach (s = 0 ... S) {
                    int idx = (b * C + c) * S + s;
                    float normalized = (input[idx] - mean) * inv_std;
                    output[idx] = normalized * gamma[c] + beta[c];
                }
            }
        }
    } else {
        for (uniform int c = 0; c < C; c++) {
            uniform float mean = running_mean[c];
            uniform float var = running_var[c];
            uniform float inv_std = fast_rsqrt(var + eps);

            for (uniform int b = 0; b < B; b++) {
                foreach (s = 0 ... S) {
                    int idx = (b * C + c) * S + s;
                    float normalized = (input[idx] - mean) * inv_std;
                    output[idx] = normalized * gamma[c] + beta[c];
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

export void embedding_forward(
    uniform float output[],
    uniform int indices[],
    uniform float embedding_table[],
    uniform int batch_size,
    uniform int seq_length,
    uniform int embedding_dim
) {
    for (uniform int b = 0; b < batch_size; b++) {
        for (uniform int s = 0; s < seq_length; s++) {
            uniform int idx = indices[b * seq_length + s];
            uniform float * uniform emb = embedding_table + idx * embedding_dim;
            uniform float * uniform out = output + (b * seq_length + s) * embedding_dim;

            foreach (d = 0 ... embedding_dim) {
                out[d] = emb[d];
            }
        }
    }
}

export void rotary_embedding(
    uniform float output[],
    uniform float input[],
    uniform float cos_cache[],
    uniform float sin_cache[],
    uniform int batch_size,
    uniform int num_heads,
    uniform int seq_length,
    uniform int head_dim
) {
    uniform int half_dim = head_dim / 2;
    uniform int head_stride = seq_length * head_dim;
    uniform int batch_stride = num_heads * head_stride;

    for (uniform int b = 0; b < batch_size; b++) {
        for (uniform int h = 0; h < num_heads; h++) {
            for (uniform int s = 0; s < seq_length; s++) {
                uniform float * uniform x = input + b * batch_stride + h * head_stride + s * head_dim;
                uniform float * uniform y = output + b * batch_stride + h * head_stride + s * head_dim;
                uniform float * uniform cos_ptr = cos_cache + s * half_dim;
                uniform float * uniform sin_ptr = sin_cache + s * half_dim;

                foreach (d = 0 ... half_dim) {
                    float x1 = x[d];
                    float x2 = x[d + half_dim];
                    float cos_val = cos_ptr[d];
                    float sin_val = sin_ptr[d];

                    y[d] = x1 * cos_val - x2 * sin_val;
                    y[d + half_dim] = x1 * sin_val + x2 * cos_val;
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

export void dropout_forward(
    uniform float output[],
    uniform float input[],
    uniform float mask[],
    uniform float scale,
    uniform int size
) {
    foreach (i = 0 ... size) {
        output[i] = input[i] * mask[i] * scale;
    }
}

export void cross_entropy_loss(
    uniform float loss[],
    uniform float grad[],
    uniform float logits[],
    uniform int targets[],
    uniform int batch_size,
    uniform int num_classes
) {
    for (uniform int b = 0; b < batch_size; b++) {
        uniform float * uniform logit = logits + b * num_classes;
        uniform int target = targets[b];

        float max_logit = logit[0];
        for (uniform int c = 1; c < num_classes; c++) {
            max_logit = max(max_logit, logit[c]);
        }
        uniform float max_val = reduce_max(max_logit);

        float sum_exp = 0.0f;
        foreach (c = 0 ... num_classes) {
            sum_exp += fast_exp(logit[c] - max_val);
        }
        uniform float log_sum_exp = log(reduce_add(sum_exp)) + max_val;

        loss[b] = log_sum_exp - logit[target];

        if (grad != NULL) {
            uniform float * uniform g = grad + b * num_classes;
            foreach (c = 0 ... num_classes) {
                float prob = fast_exp(logit[c] - log_sum_exp);
                g[c] = prob;
            }
            g[target] -= 1.0f;
        }
    }
}

export void adam_update(
    uniform float params[],
    uniform float grads[],
    uniform float m[],
    uniform float v[],
    uniform float lr,
    uniform float beta1,
    uniform float beta2,
    uniform float epsilon,
    uniform float weight_decay,
    uniform int t,
    uniform int size
) {
    uniform float beta1_t = 1.0f;
    uniform float beta2_t = 1.0f;
    for (uniform int i = 0; i < t; i++) {
        beta1_t *= beta1;
        beta2_t *= beta2;
    }
    uniform float bias_correction1 = 1.0f - beta1_t;
    uniform float bias_correction2 = 1.0f - beta2_t;

    foreach (i = 0 ... size) {
        float g = grads[i];
        if (weight_decay != 0.0f) {
            g += weight_decay * params[i];
        }

        float m_i = beta1 * m[i] + (1.0f - beta1) * g;
        float v_i = beta2 * v[i] + (1.0f - beta2) * g * g;

        m[i] = m_i;
        v[i] = v_i;

        float m_hat = m_i / bias_correction1;
        float v_hat = v_i / bias_correction2;

        params[i] -= lr * m_hat / (sqrt(v_hat) + epsilon);
    }
}

export void sgd_momentum_update(
    uniform float params[],
    uniform float grads[],
    uniform float velocity[],
    uniform float lr,
    uniform float momentum,
    uniform float weight_decay,
    uniform float dampening,
    uniform int nesterov,
    uniform int size
) {
    foreach (i = 0 ... size) {
        float g = grads[i];
        if (weight_decay != 0.0f) {
            g += weight_decay * params[i];
        }

        float v_i = momentum * velocity[i] + (1.0f - dampening) * g;
        velocity[i] = v_i;

        float update;
        if (nesterov) {
            update = g + momentum * v_i;
        } else {
            update = v_i;
        }

        params[i] -= lr * update;
    }
}

export uniform float reduce_sum(uniform float input[], uniform int size) {
    float sum = 0.0f;
    foreach (i = 0 ... size) {
        sum += input[i];
    }
    return reduce_add(sum);
}

export uniform float reduce_max_val(uniform float input[], uniform int size) {
    float max_val = input[0];
    foreach (i = 1 ... size) {
        max_val = max(max_val, input[i]);
    }
    return reduce_max(max_val);
}

export uniform float reduce_min_val(uniform float input[], uniform int size) {
    float min_val = input[0];
    foreach (i = 1 ... size) {
        min_val = min(min_val, input[i]);
    }
    return reduce_min(min_val);
}

export void transpose_2d(
    uniform float output[],
    uniform float input[],
    uniform int rows,
    uniform int cols
) {
    uniform int BLOCK = 16;

    for (uniform int i0 = 0; i0 < rows; i0 += BLOCK) {
        for (uniform int j0 = 0; j0 < cols; j0 += BLOCK) {
            uniform int i_end = min(i0 + BLOCK, rows);
            uniform int j_end = min(j0 + BLOCK, cols);

            for (uniform int i = i0; i < i_end; i++) {
                foreach (j = j0 ... j_end) {
                    output[j * rows + i] = input[i * cols + j];
                }
            }
        }
    }
}

export void concat_tensors(
    uniform float output[],
    uniform float * uniform inputs[],
    uniform int input_sizes[],
    uniform int num_inputs,
    uniform int batch_size,
    uniform int axis_dim[]
) {
    uniform int total_offset = 0;

    for (uniform int n = 0; n < num_inputs; n++) {
        uniform float * uniform src = inputs[n];
        uniform int src_size = input_sizes[n];

        foreach (i = 0 ... src_size) {
            output[total_offset + i] = src[i];
        }

        total_offset += src_size;
    }
}

export void split_tensor(
    uniform float * uniform outputs[],
    uniform float input[],
    uniform int output_sizes[],
    uniform int num_outputs
) {
    uniform int offset = 0;

    for (uniform int n = 0; n < num_outputs; n++) {
        uniform float * uniform dst = outputs[n];
        uniform int size = output_sizes[n];

        foreach (i = 0 ... size) {
            dst[i] = input[offset + i];
        }

        offset += size;
    }
}

export void broadcast_add(
    uniform float output[],
    uniform float input[],
    uniform float bias[],
    uniform int batch_size,
    uniform int channels,
    uniform int spatial_size
) {
    for (uniform int b = 0; b < batch_size; b++) {
        for (uniform int c = 0; c < channels; c++) {
            uniform int offset = (b * channels + c) * spatial_size;
            uniform float b_val = bias[c];

            foreach (s = 0 ... spatial_size) {
                output[offset + s] = input[offset + s] + b_val;
            }
        }
    }
}

export void broadcast_multiply(
    uniform float output[],
    uniform float input[],
    uniform float scale[],
    uniform int batch_size,
    uniform int channels,
    uniform int spatial_size
) {
    for (uniform int b = 0; b < batch_size; b++) {
        for (uniform int c = 0; c < channels; c++) {
            uniform int offset = (b * channels + c) * spatial_size;
            uniform float s_val = scale[c];

            foreach (s = 0 ... spatial_size) {
                output[offset + s] = input[offset + s] * s_val;
            }
        }
    }
}

export void clip_gradient(
    uniform float grads[],
    uniform float max_norm,
    uniform int size
) {
    float sum_sq = 0.0f;
    foreach (i = 0 ... size) {
        float g = grads[i];
        sum_sq += g * g;
    }
    uniform float total_norm = sqrt(reduce_add(sum_sq));

    if (total_norm > max_norm) {
        uniform float scale = max_norm / total_norm;
        foreach (i = 0 ... size) {
            grads[i] *= scale;
        }
    }
}

File: ./runtime/scopes_runtime.sc
using import struct
using import enum
using import Array
using import Map
using import String
using import Option
using import itertools

enum TensorDType
    Float32
    Float16
    BFloat16
    Int32
    Int64
    Int8
    UInt8

struct TensorShape
    dims : (Array i32)
    ndim : i32
    
    inline __typecall (cls dims...)
        local shape =
            Struct.__typecall cls
                dims = (Array i32)
                ndim = ((va-countof dims) as i32)
        for i dim in (enumerate dims...)
            'append shape.dims (dim as i32)
        shape

    fn size (self)
        local result = 1:i32
        for d in self.dims
            result *= d
        result

    fn equals (self other)
        if (self.ndim != other.ndim)
            return false
        for i in (range self.ndim)
            if ((self.dims @ i) != (other.dims @ i))
                return false
        true

struct Tensor
    data : (Array f32)
    shape : TensorShape
    dtype : TensorDType
    requires_grad : bool
    grad : (Option (Array f32))
    
    inline __typecall (cls shape)
        local size = ('size shape)
        local data = (Array f32)
        for i in (range size)
            'append data 0.0:f32
        Struct.__typecall cls
            data = data
            shape = shape
            dtype = TensorDType.Float32
            requires_grad = false
            grad = (Option (Array f32))

    fn fill (self value)
        for i in (range (countof self.data))
            self.data @ i = value

    fn clone (self)
        local new_tensor = (Tensor self.shape)
        for i in (range (countof self.data))
            new_tensor.data @ i = (self.data @ i)
        new_tensor.dtype = self.dtype
        new_tensor.requires_grad = self.requires_grad
        new_tensor

    fn zero_grad (self)
        match self.grad
            case Some (g)
                for i in (range (countof g))
                    g @ i = 0.0:f32
            default
                ;

enum LayerType
    Linear
    Conv2d
    BatchNorm
    LayerNorm
    RMSNorm
    ReLU
    GELU
    SiLU
    Softmax
    Dropout
    Embedding
    Attention

struct LayerConfig
    layer_type : LayerType
    in_features : i32
    out_features : i32
    num_heads : i32
    head_dim : i32
    epsilon : f32
    bias : bool
    dropout_p : f32
    
    inline __typecall (cls ltype in_f out_f)
        Struct.__typecall cls
            layer_type = ltype
            in_features = in_f
            out_features = out_f
            num_heads = 1
            head_dim = 64
            epsilon = 1.0e-5:f32
            bias = true
            dropout_p = 0.0:f32

struct Layer
    config : LayerConfig
    weight : (Option Tensor)
    bias : (Option Tensor)
    gamma : (Option Tensor)
    beta : (Option Tensor)
    
    fn forward (self input)
        switch self.config.layer_type
        case LayerType.Linear
            forward_linear self input
        case LayerType.ReLU
            forward_relu self input
        case LayerType.GELU
            forward_gelu self input
        case LayerType.SiLU
            forward_silu self input
        case LayerType.Softmax
            forward_softmax self input
        case LayerType.LayerNorm
            forward_layer_norm self input
        case LayerType.RMSNorm
            forward_rms_norm self input
        default
            'clone input

    fn forward_linear (self input)
        local batch_size = (input.shape.dims @ 0)
        local in_features = self.config.in_features
        local out_features = self.config.out_features
        
        local output_shape = (TensorShape batch_size out_features)
        local output = (Tensor output_shape)
        
        match self.weight
            case Some (w)
                for b in (range batch_size)
                    for o in (range out_features)
                        local sum = 0.0:f32
                        for i in (range in_features)
                            local input_idx = (b * in_features + i)
                            local weight_idx = (o * in_features + i)
                            sum += (input.data @ input_idx) * (w.data @ weight_idx)
                        
                        match self.bias
                            case Some (bias_tensor)
                                sum += (bias_tensor.data @ o)
                            default
                                ;
                        
                        local output_idx = (b * out_features + o)
                        output.data @ output_idx = sum
            default
                ;
        
        output

    fn forward_relu (self input)
        local output = ('clone input)
        for i in (range (countof output.data))
            local val = (output.data @ i)
            if (val < 0.0:f32)
                output.data @ i = 0.0:f32
        output

    fn forward_gelu (self input)
        local output = ('clone input)
        for i in (range (countof output.data))
            local x = (output.data @ i)
            local x3 = x * x * x
            local inner = 0.797884560803:f32 * (x + 0.044715:f32 * x3)
            local tanh_val = (tanh inner)
            output.data @ i = 0.5:f32 * x * (1.0:f32 + tanh_val)
        output

    fn forward_silu (self input)
        local output = ('clone input)
        for i in (range (countof output.data))
            local x = (output.data @ i)
            local sigmoid_x = 1.0:f32 / (1.0:f32 + (exp (- x)))
            output.data @ i = x * sigmoid_x
        output

    fn forward_softmax (self input)
        local batch_size = (input.shape.dims @ 0)
        local num_classes = (input.shape.dims @ 1)
        
        local output = ('clone input)
        
        for b in (range batch_size)
            local max_val = (input.data @ (b * num_classes))
            for c in (range 1 num_classes)
                local idx = (b * num_classes + c)
                local val = (input.data @ idx)
                if (val > max_val)
                    max_val = val
            
            local sum_exp = 0.0:f32
            for c in (range num_classes)
                local idx = (b * num_classes + c)
                local exp_val = (exp ((input.data @ idx) - max_val))
                output.data @ idx = exp_val
                sum_exp += exp_val
            
            for c in (range num_classes)
                local idx = (b * num_classes + c)
                output.data @ idx = (output.data @ idx) / sum_exp
        
        output

    fn forward_layer_norm (self input)
        local batch_size = (input.shape.dims @ 0)
        local hidden_size = self.config.in_features
        local epsilon = self.config.epsilon
        
        local output = ('clone input)
        
        for b in (range batch_size)
            local sum = 0.0:f32
            for h in (range hidden_size)
                local idx = (b * hidden_size + h)
                sum += (input.data @ idx)
            local mean = sum / (hidden_size as f32)
            
            local var_sum = 0.0:f32
            for h in (range hidden_size)
                local idx = (b * hidden_size + h)
                local diff = (input.data @ idx) - mean
                var_sum += diff * diff
            local variance = var_sum / (hidden_size as f32)
            local inv_std = 1.0:f32 / (sqrt (variance + epsilon))
            
            for h in (range hidden_size)
                local idx = (b * hidden_size + h)
                local normalized = ((input.data @ idx) - mean) * inv_std
                
                match self.gamma
                    case Some (g)
                        normalized *= (g.data @ h)
                    default
                        ;
                
                match self.beta
                    case Some (bt)
                        normalized += (bt.data @ h)
                    default
                        ;
                
                output.data @ idx = normalized
        
        output

    fn forward_rms_norm (self input)
        local batch_size = (input.shape.dims @ 0)
        local hidden_size = self.config.in_features
        local epsilon = self.config.epsilon
        
        local output = ('clone input)
        
        for b in (range batch_size)
            local sum_sq = 0.0:f32
            for h in (range hidden_size)
                local idx = (b * hidden_size + h)
                local x = (input.data @ idx)
                sum_sq += x * x
            local rms = 1.0:f32 / (sqrt (sum_sq / (hidden_size as f32) + epsilon))
            
            for h in (range hidden_size)
                local idx = (b * hidden_size + h)
                local result = (input.data @ idx) * rms
                
                match self.gamma
                    case Some (g)
                        result *= (g.data @ h)
                    default
                        ;
                
                output.data @ idx = result
        
        output

struct ComputeGraph
    layers : (Array Layer)
    layer_count : i32
    
    inline __typecall (cls)
        Struct.__typecall cls
            layers = (Array Layer)
            layer_count = 0

    fn add_layer (self config)
        local layer =
            Struct.__typecall Layer
                config = config
                weight = (Option Tensor)
                bias = (Option Tensor)
                gamma = (Option Tensor)
                beta = (Option Tensor)
        'append self.layers layer
        self.layer_count += 1

    fn forward (self input)
        local current = ('clone input)
        for layer in self.layers
            current = ('forward layer current)
        current

enum OptimizerType
    SGD
    Adam
    AdamW
    RMSprop

struct OptimizerConfig
    optimizer_type : OptimizerType
    learning_rate : f32
    momentum : f32
    beta1 : f32
    beta2 : f32
    epsilon : f32
    weight_decay : f32
    
    inline __typecall (cls opt_type lr)
        Struct.__typecall cls
            optimizer_type = opt_type
            learning_rate = lr
            momentum = 0.9:f32
            beta1 = 0.9:f32
            beta2 = 0.999:f32
            epsilon = 1.0e-8:f32
            weight_decay = 0.0:f32

struct ParameterState
    exp_avg : (Array f32)
    exp_avg_sq : (Array f32)
    step : i32
    
    inline __typecall (cls size)
        local exp_avg = (Array f32)
        local exp_avg_sq = (Array f32)
        for i in (range size)
            'append exp_avg 0.0:f32
            'append exp_avg_sq 0.0:f32
        Struct.__typecall cls
            exp_avg = exp_avg
            exp_avg_sq = exp_avg_sq
            step = 0

struct Optimizer
    config : OptimizerConfig
    states : (Array ParameterState)
    
    fn step (self params grads)
        switch self.config.optimizer_type
        case OptimizerType.SGD
            step_sgd self params grads
        case OptimizerType.Adam
            step_adam self params grads
        case OptimizerType.AdamW
            step_adamw self params grads
        default
            ;

    fn step_sgd (self params grads)
        local lr = self.config.learning_rate
        local momentum = self.config.momentum
        local wd = self.config.weight_decay
        
        for i state in (enumerate self.states)
            local param = (params @ i)
            local grad = (grads @ i)
            
            for j in (range (countof param.data))
                local g = (grad.data @ j)
                if (wd != 0.0:f32)
                    g += wd * (param.data @ j)
                
                if (momentum != 0.0:f32)
                    if (state.step == 0)
                        state.exp_avg @ j = g
                    else
                        state.exp_avg @ j = momentum * (state.exp_avg @ j) + g
                    g = (state.exp_avg @ j)
                
                param.data @ j = (param.data @ j) - lr * g
            
            state.step += 1

    fn step_adam (self params grads)
        local lr = self.config.learning_rate
        local beta1 = self.config.beta1
        local beta2 = self.config.beta2
        local eps = self.config.epsilon
        local wd = self.config.weight_decay
        
        for i state in (enumerate self.states)
            local param = (params @ i)
            local grad = (grads @ i)
            
            state.step += 1
            
            local bias_correction1 = 1.0:f32 - (pow beta1 (state.step as f32))
            local bias_correction2 = 1.0:f32 - (pow beta2 (state.step as f32))
            
            for j in (range (countof param.data))
                local g = (grad.data @ j)
                if (wd != 0.0:f32)
                    g += wd * (param.data @ j)
                
                state.exp_avg @ j = beta1 * (state.exp_avg @ j) + (1.0:f32 - beta1) * g
                state.exp_avg_sq @ j = beta2 * (state.exp_avg_sq @ j) + (1.0:f32 - beta2) * g * g
                
                local m_hat = (state.exp_avg @ j) / bias_correction1
                local v_hat = (state.exp_avg_sq @ j) / bias_correction2
                
                param.data @ j = (param.data @ j) - lr * m_hat / ((sqrt v_hat) + eps)

    fn step_adamw (self params grads)
        local lr = self.config.learning_rate
        local beta1 = self.config.beta1
        local beta2 = self.config.beta2
        local eps = self.config.epsilon
        local wd = self.config.weight_decay
        
        for i state in (enumerate self.states)
            local param = (params @ i)
            local grad = (grads @ i)
            
            for j in (range (countof param.data))
                param.data @ j = (param.data @ j) * (1.0:f32 - lr * wd)
            
            state.step += 1
            
            local bias_correction1 = 1.0:f32 - (pow beta1 (state.step as f32))
            local bias_correction2 = 1.0:f32 - (pow beta2 (state.step as f32))
            
            for j in (range (countof param.data))
                local g = (grad.data @ j)
                
                state.exp_avg @ j = beta1 * (state.exp_avg @ j) + (1.0:f32 - beta1) * g
                state.exp_avg_sq @ j = beta2 * (state.exp_avg_sq @ j) + (1.0:f32 - beta2) * g * g
                
                local m_hat = (state.exp_avg @ j) / bias_correction1
                local v_hat = (state.exp_avg_sq @ j) / bias_correction2
                
                param.data @ j = (param.data @ j) - lr * m_hat / ((sqrt v_hat) + eps)

struct LRScheduler
    base_lr : f32
    current_lr : f32
    step_count : i32
    total_steps : i32
    warmup_steps : i32
    min_lr : f32
    
    inline __typecall (cls base_lr total warmup)
        Struct.__typecall cls
            base_lr = base_lr
            current_lr = 0.0:f32
            step_count = 0
            total_steps = total
            warmup_steps = warmup
            min_lr = 0.0:f32

    fn step (self)
        self.step_count += 1
        
        if (self.step_count <= self.warmup_steps)
            self.current_lr = self.base_lr * ((self.step_count as f32) / (self.warmup_steps as f32))
        else
            local progress = ((self.step_count - self.warmup_steps) as f32) / ((self.total_steps - self.warmup_steps) as f32)
            local cos_inner = 3.14159265359:f32 * progress
            self.current_lr = self.min_lr + (self.base_lr - self.min_lr) * (1.0:f32 + (cos cos_inner)) / 2.0:f32
        
        self.current_lr

    fn get_lr (self)
        self.current_lr

struct KVCache
    keys : (Array Tensor)
    values : (Array Tensor)
    sequence_length : i32
    max_length : i32
    
    inline __typecall (cls num_layers max_len num_heads head_dim)
        local keys = (Array Tensor)
        local values = (Array Tensor)
        
        for l in (range num_layers)
            local key_shape = (TensorShape 1 max_len num_heads head_dim)
            local value_shape = (TensorShape 1 max_len num_heads head_dim)
            'append keys (Tensor key_shape)
            'append values (Tensor value_shape)
        
        Struct.__typecall cls
            keys = keys
            values = values
            sequence_length = 0
            max_length = max_len

    fn reset (self)
        self.sequence_length = 0

    fn append (self layer_idx new_keys new_values)
        for i in (range (countof new_keys.data))
            local dst_offset = self.sequence_length * (countof new_keys.data)
            (self.keys @ layer_idx).data @ (dst_offset + i) = (new_keys.data @ i)
            (self.values @ layer_idx).data @ (dst_offset + i) = (new_values.data @ i)
        self.sequence_length += 1

struct InferenceEngine
    graph : ComputeGraph
    kv_cache : (Option KVCache)
    is_initialized : bool
    
    inline __typecall (cls)
        Struct.__typecall cls
            graph = (ComputeGraph)
            kv_cache = (Option KVCache)
            is_initialized = false

    fn add_layer (self config)
        'add_layer self.graph config

    fn forward (self input)
        'forward self.graph input

    fn generate (self input_ids max_tokens temperature top_p)
        local current_ids = input_ids
        
        for t in (range max_tokens)
            local logits = ('forward self current_ids)
            local next_token = (sample_token logits temperature top_p)
            'append current_ids.data (next_token as f32)
        
        current_ids

fn sample_token (logits temperature top_p)
    local vocab_size = (logits.shape.dims @ 1)
    local last_offset = ((countof logits.data) - vocab_size)
    
    local max_logit = (logits.data @ last_offset)
    for i in (range 1 vocab_size)
        local val = (logits.data @ (last_offset + i))
        if (val > max_logit)
            max_logit = val
    
    local sum_exp = 0.0:f32
    for i in (range vocab_size)
        local idx = (last_offset + i)
        local exp_val = (exp ((logits.data @ idx) - max_logit) / temperature)
        logits.data @ idx = exp_val
        sum_exp += exp_val
    
    for i in (range vocab_size)
        local idx = (last_offset + i)
        logits.data @ idx = (logits.data @ idx) / sum_exp
    
    0:i32

fn cross_entropy_loss (logits targets)
    local batch_size = (logits.shape.dims @ 0)
    local num_classes = (logits.shape.dims @ 1)
    
    local total_loss = 0.0:f32
    
    for b in (range batch_size)
        local target = (targets.data @ b) as i32
        
        local max_logit = (logits.data @ (b * num_classes))
        for c in (range 1 num_classes)
            local val = (logits.data @ (b * num_classes + c))
            if (val > max_logit)
                max_logit = val
        
        local sum_exp = 0.0:f32
        for c in (range num_classes)
            sum_exp += (exp ((logits.data @ (b * num_classes + c)) - max_logit))
        
        local log_softmax = (logits.data @ (b * num_classes + target)) - max_logit - (log sum_exp)
        total_loss -= log_softmax
    
    total_loss / (batch_size as f32)

fn mse_loss (predictions targets)
    local size = ('size predictions.shape)
    local total_loss = 0.0:f32
    
    for i in (range size)
        local diff = (predictions.data @ i) - (targets.data @ i)
        total_loss += diff * diff
    
    total_loss / (size as f32)

fn clip_gradient_norm (grads max_norm)
    local total_norm = 0.0:f32
    
    for grad in grads
        for i in (range (countof grad.data))
            local g = (grad.data @ i)
            total_norm += g * g
    
    total_norm = (sqrt total_norm)
    
    if (total_norm > max_norm)
        local scale = max_norm / total_norm
        for grad in grads
            for i in (range (countof grad.data))
                grad.data @ i = (grad.data @ i) * scale
    
    total_norm

fn main ()
    local input_shape = (TensorShape 2 768)
    local input = (Tensor input_shape)
    'fill input 0.5:f32
    
    local graph = (ComputeGraph)
    
    local linear_config = (LayerConfig LayerType.Linear 768 256)
    'add_layer graph linear_config
    
    local relu_config = (LayerConfig LayerType.ReLU 256 256)
    'add_layer graph relu_config
    
    local output_config = (LayerConfig LayerType.Linear 256 10)
    'add_layer graph output_config
    
    local softmax_config = (LayerConfig LayerType.Softmax 10 10)
    'add_layer graph softmax_config
    
    local output = ('forward graph input)
    
    print "Neural framework runtime initialized"
    0

import std.channel (Channel, Sender, Receiver)
import std.process (Process)
import std.string (String, StringBuffer)
import std.array (Array)
import std.hash (Hash, Hasher)
import std.map (Map)
import std.set (Set)
import std.option (Option, Some, None)
import std.result (Result, Ok, Err)
import std.iter (Iterator)
import std.io (Write, Read, ByteWriter, ByteReader)
import std.fs (File, Path, Directory)
import std.time (Duration, Instant)
