}

File: ./data_loader/parallel_loader.inko
import std.channel (Channel, Sender, Receiver)
import std.process (Process)
import std.string (String, StringBuffer)
import std.array (Array)
import std.hash (Hash, Hasher)
import std.map (Map)
import std.set (Set)
import std.option (Option, Some, None)
import std.result (Result, Ok, Err)
import std.iter (Iterator)
import std.io (Write, Read)
import std.fs (File, Path, Directory)
import std.time (Duration, Instant)
import std.sync (Mutex, RwLock)
import std.cmp (Ordering, Compare)
import std.fmt (Format, Formatter)
import std.rand (Random)
import std.bytes (Bytes)

class DataSample {
    let @id: Int
    let @data: Array[Float]
    let @label: Int
    let @features: Map[String, Float]
    let @metadata: Map[String, String]
    let @weight: Float
    let @is_valid: Bool

    fn static new(id: Int, data: Array[Float], label: Int) -> DataSample {
        DataSample {
            @id = id,
            @data = data,
            @label = label,
            @features = Map.new,
            @metadata = Map.new,
            @weight = 1.0,
            @is_valid = true
        }
    }

    fn with_features(mut self, features: Map[String, Float]) -> DataSample {
        @features = features
        self
    }

    fn with_metadata(mut self, metadata: Map[String, String]) -> DataSample {
        @metadata = metadata
        self
    }

    fn with_weight(mut self, weight: Float) -> DataSample {
        @weight = weight
        self
    }

    fn data_size -> Int {
        @data.size
    }

    fn clone -> DataSample {
        DataSample {
            @id = @id,
            @data = @data.clone,
            @label = @label,
            @features = @features.clone,
            @metadata = @metadata.clone,
            @weight = @weight,
            @is_valid = @is_valid
        }
    }
}

class Batch {
    let @batch_id: Int
    let @samples: Array[DataSample]
    let @batch_size: Int
    let @data_tensor: Array[Float]
    let @label_tensor: Array[Int]
    let @attention_mask: Array[Float]
    let @is_padded: Bool
    let @creation_time: Instant

    fn static new(batch_id: Int, samples: Array[DataSample]) -> Batch {
        let batch_size = samples.size
        let mut data_tensor = Array.new
        let mut label_tensor = Array.new
        let mut attention_mask = Array.new

        let mut i = 0
        loop {
            if i >= batch_size {
                break
            }
            let sample = samples.get(i).unwrap
            
            let mut j = 0
            loop {
                if j >= sample.data.size {
                    break
                }
                data_tensor.push(sample.data.get(j).unwrap)
                attention_mask.push(1.0)
                j = j + 1
            }
            
            label_tensor.push(sample.label)
            i = i + 1
        }

        Batch {
            @batch_id = batch_id,
            @samples = samples,
            @batch_size = batch_size,
            @data_tensor = data_tensor,
            @label_tensor = label_tensor,
            @attention_mask = attention_mask,
            @is_padded = false,
            @creation_time = Instant.now
        }
    }

    fn pad_to_length(mut self, target_length: Int, pad_value: Float) {
        let current_length = @data_tensor.size / @batch_size
        if current_length >= target_length {
            return
        }

        let mut new_data = Array.new
        let mut new_mask = Array.new

        let mut b = 0
        loop {
            if b >= @batch_size {
                break
            }
            
            let mut i = 0
            loop {
                if i >= target_length {
                    break
                }
                if i < current_length {
                    new_data.push(@data_tensor.get(b * current_length + i).unwrap)
                    new_mask.push(1.0)
                } else {
                    new_data.push(pad_value)
                    new_mask.push(0.0)
                }
                i = i + 1
            }
            
            b = b + 1
        }

        @data_tensor = new_data
        @attention_mask = new_mask
        @is_padded = true
    }
}

class DatasetConfig {
    let @batch_size: Int
    let @shuffle: Bool
    let @num_workers: Int
    let @prefetch_factor: Int
    let @drop_last: Bool
    let @pin_memory: Bool
    let @persistent_workers: Bool
    let @seed: Int
    let @max_samples: Int
    let @validation_split: Float
    let @augmentation_enabled: Bool

    fn static default -> DatasetConfig {
        DatasetConfig {
            @batch_size = 32,
            @shuffle = true,
            @num_workers = 4,
            @prefetch_factor = 2,
            @drop_last = false,
            @pin_memory = true,
            @persistent_workers = true,
            @seed = 42,
            @max_samples = -1,
            @validation_split = 0.1,
            @augmentation_enabled = true
        }
    }

    fn with_batch_size(mut self, size: Int) -> DatasetConfig {
        @batch_size = size
        self
    }

    fn with_num_workers(mut self, workers: Int) -> DatasetConfig {
        @num_workers = workers
        self
    }

    fn with_shuffle(mut self, shuffle: Bool) -> DatasetConfig {
        @shuffle = shuffle
        self
    }
}

class LoaderMessage {
    let @message_type: Int
    let @batch_indices: Array[Int]
    let @worker_id: Int
    let @priority: Int

    fn static load_batch(indices: Array[Int], priority: Int) -> LoaderMessage {
        LoaderMessage {
            @message_type = 0,
            @batch_indices = indices,
            @worker_id = -1,
            @priority = priority
        }
    }

    fn static shutdown -> LoaderMessage {
        LoaderMessage {
            @message_type = -1,
            @batch_indices = Array.new,
            @worker_id = -1,
            @priority = 0
        }
    }

    fn static prefetch(indices: Array[Int]) -> LoaderMessage {
        LoaderMessage {
            @message_type = 1,
            @batch_indices = indices,
            @worker_id = -1,
            @priority = 1
        }
    }
}

class LoaderResult {
    let @batch: Batch
    let @worker_id: Int
    let @load_time_ns: Int
    let @success: Bool
    let @error_message: String
    let @cache_hit: Bool

    fn static success(batch: Batch, worker_id: Int, load_time: Int) -> LoaderResult {
        LoaderResult {
            @batch = batch,
            @worker_id = worker_id,
            @load_time_ns = load_time,
            @success = true,
            @error_message = "",
            @cache_hit = false
        }
    }

    fn static failure(error: String, worker_id: Int) -> LoaderResult {
        LoaderResult {
            @batch = Batch.new(0, Array.new),
            @worker_id = worker_id,
            @load_time_ns = 0,
            @success = false,
            @error_message = error,
            @cache_hit = false
        }
    }
}

class DataAugmentation {
    let @random_flip_horizontal: Bool
    let @random_flip_vertical: Bool
    let @random_rotation: Bool
    let @rotation_degrees: Float
    let @random_crop: Bool
    let @crop_size: Int
    let @normalize: Bool
    let @mean: Array[Float]
    let @std: Array[Float]
    let @noise_factor: Float
    let @mixup_alpha: Float
    let @cutout_size: Int

    fn static default -> DataAugmentation {
        DataAugmentation {
            @random_flip_horizontal = true,
            @random_flip_vertical = false,
            @random_rotation = true,
            @rotation_degrees = 15.0,
            @random_crop = true,
            @crop_size = 224,
            @normalize = true,
            @mean = [0.485, 0.456, 0.406],
            @std = [0.229, 0.224, 0.225],
            @noise_factor = 0.0,
            @mixup_alpha = 0.0,
            @cutout_size = 0
        }
    }

    fn apply(data: Array[Float], rng: ref Random) -> Array[Float] {
        let mut result = data.clone

        if @normalize {
            result = normalize_data(result)
        }

        if @noise_factor > 0.0 {
            result = add_noise(result, rng)
        }

        result
    }

    fn normalize_data(data: Array[Float]) -> Array[Float] {
        let mut result = Array.new
        let num_channels = @mean.size
        let spatial_size = data.size / num_channels

        let mut c = 0
        loop {
            if c >= num_channels {
                break
            }
            let mean_c = @mean.get(c).unwrap
            let std_c = @std.get(c).unwrap

            let mut i = 0
            loop {
                if i >= spatial_size {
                    break
                }
                let idx = c * spatial_size + i
                let val = data.get(idx).unwrap
                result.push((val - mean_c) / std_c)
                i = i + 1
            }
            c = c + 1
        }

        result
    }

    fn add_noise(data: Array[Float], rng: ref Random) -> Array[Float] {
        let mut result = Array.new

        let mut i = 0
        loop {
            if i >= data.size {
                break
            }
            let val = data.get(i).unwrap
            let noise = (rng.float - 0.5) * 2.0 * @noise_factor
            result.push(val + noise)
            i = i + 1
        }

        result
    }
}

class SampleCache {
    let @cache: Map[Int, DataSample]
    let @max_size: Int
    let @access_order: Array[Int]
    let @hits: Int
    let @misses: Int

    fn static new(max_size: Int) -> SampleCache {
        SampleCache {
            @cache = Map.new,
            @max_size = max_size,
            @access_order = Array.new,
            @hits = 0,
            @misses = 0
        }
    }

    fn mut get(key: Int) -> Option[DataSample] {
        match @cache.get(key) {
            case Some(sample) -> {
                @hits = @hits + 1
                update_access(key)
                Some(sample.clone)
            }
            case None -> {
                @misses = @misses + 1
                None
            }
        }
    }

    fn mut put(key: Int, sample: DataSample) {
        if @cache.size >= @max_size {
            evict_lru
        }
        @cache.set(key, sample)
        @access_order.push(key)
    }

    fn mut update_access(key: Int) {
        let mut new_order = Array.new
        let mut i = 0
        loop {
            if i >= @access_order.size {
                break
            }
            let k = @access_order.get(i).unwrap
            if k != key {
                new_order.push(k)
            }
            i = i + 1
        }
        new_order.push(key)
        @access_order = new_order
    }

    fn mut evict_lru {
        if @access_order.size > 0 {
            let lru_key = @access_order.get(0).unwrap
            @cache.remove(lru_key)
            let mut new_order = Array.new
            let mut i = 1
            loop {
                if i >= @access_order.size {
                    break
                }
                new_order.push(@access_order.get(i).unwrap)
                i = i + 1
            }
            @access_order = new_order
        }
    }

    fn hit_rate -> Float {
        let total = @hits + @misses
        if total == 0 {
            return 0.0
        }
        Float.from_int(@hits) / Float.from_int(total)
    }

    fn mut clear {
        @cache = Map.new
        @access_order = Array.new
        @hits = 0
        @misses = 0
    }
}

class DataLoaderWorker {
    let @worker_id: Int
    let @dataset: Array[DataSample]
    let @input_channel: Receiver[LoaderMessage]
    let @output_channel: Sender[LoaderResult]
    let @augmentation: DataAugmentation
    let @cache: SampleCache
    let @rng: Random
    let @samples_loaded: Int
    let @total_load_time: Int

    fn static spawn(
        worker_id: Int,
        dataset: Array[DataSample],
        input: Receiver[LoaderMessage],
        output: Sender[LoaderResult],
        augmentation: DataAugmentation,
        cache_size: Int,
        seed: Int
    ) -> Process {
        Process.spawn {
            let mut worker = DataLoaderWorker {
                @worker_id = worker_id,
                @dataset = dataset,
                @input_channel = input,
                @output_channel = output,
                @augmentation = augmentation,
                @cache = SampleCache.new(cache_size),
                @rng = Random.new(seed + worker_id),
                @samples_loaded = 0,
                @total_load_time = 0
            }
            worker.run
        }
    }

    fn mut run {
        loop {
            match @input_channel.receive {
                case Some(message) -> {
                    if message.message_type == -1 {
                        break
                    }
                    let result = process_message(message)
                    @output_channel.send(result)
                }
                case None -> break
            }
        }
    }

    fn mut process_message(message: LoaderMessage) -> LoaderResult {
        let start_time = Instant.now

        let indices = message.batch_indices
        let mut samples = Array.new

        let mut i = 0
        loop {
            if i >= indices.size {
                break
            }
            let idx = indices.get(i).unwrap
            
            let sample = match @cache.get(idx) {
                case Some(cached) -> cached
                case None -> {
                    if idx >= 0 and idx < @dataset.size {
                        let original = @dataset.get(idx).unwrap
                        let mut augmented = original.clone
                        augmented = DataSample {
                            @id = original.id,
                            @data = @augmentation.apply(original.data, @rng),
                            @label = original.label,
                            @features = original.features,
                            @metadata = original.metadata,
                            @weight = original.weight,
                            @is_valid = original.is_valid
                        }
                        @cache.put(idx, augmented.clone)
                        augmented
                    } else {
                        DataSample.new(-1, Array.new, -1)
                    }
                }
            }
            
            if sample.is_valid {
                samples.push(sample)
            }
            
            @samples_loaded = @samples_loaded + 1
            i = i + 1
        }

        let batch = Batch.new(message.priority, samples)
        let elapsed = start_time.elapsed
        @total_load_time = @total_load_time + elapsed.as_nanos.to_int

        LoaderResult.success(batch, @worker_id, elapsed.as_nanos.to_int)
    }
}

class IndexSampler {
    let @indices: Array[Int]
    let @shuffle: Bool
    let @seed: Int
    let @current_epoch: Int
    let @rng: Random

    fn static new(size: Int, shuffle: Bool, seed: Int) -> IndexSampler {
        let mut indices = Array.new
        let mut i = 0
        loop {
            if i >= size {
                break
            }
            indices.push(i)
            i = i + 1
        }

        let sampler = IndexSampler {
            @indices = indices,
            @shuffle = shuffle,
            @seed = seed,
            @current_epoch = 0,
            @rng = Random.new(seed)
        }

        sampler
    }

    fn mut reset_epoch {
        @current_epoch = @current_epoch + 1
        if @shuffle {
            shuffle_indices
        }
    }

    fn mut shuffle_indices {
        let n = @indices.size
        let mut i = n - 1
        loop {
            if i <= 0 {
                break
            }
            let j = @rng.int_max(i + 1)
            let temp = @indices.get(i).unwrap
            @indices.set(i, @indices.get(j).unwrap)
            @indices.set(j, temp)
            i = i - 1
        }
    }

    fn get_batch_indices(batch_idx: Int, batch_size: Int) -> Array[Int] {
        let start = batch_idx * batch_size
        let end = min(start + batch_size, @indices.size)
        
        let mut result = Array.new
        let mut i = start
        loop {
            if i >= end {
                break
            }
            result.push(@indices.get(i).unwrap)
            i = i + 1
        }
        result
    }

    fn num_batches(batch_size: Int, drop_last: Bool) -> Int {
        if drop_last {
            @indices.size / batch_size
        } else {
            (@indices.size + batch_size - 1) / batch_size
        }
    }
}

fn min(a: Int, b: Int) -> Int {
    if a < b { a } else { b }
}

class ParallelDataLoader {
    let @config: DatasetConfig
    let @dataset: Array[DataSample]
    let @sampler: IndexSampler
    let @workers: Array[Process]
    let @input_channels: Array[Sender[LoaderMessage]]
    let @output_channel: Receiver[LoaderResult]
    let @output_sender: Sender[LoaderResult]
    let @prefetch_queue: Array[Int]
    let @current_batch_idx: Int
    let @epoch: Int
    let @augmentation: DataAugmentation
    let @stats: LoaderStats

    fn static new(dataset: Array[DataSample], config: DatasetConfig) -> ParallelDataLoader {
        let (output_sender, output_receiver) = Channel.new

        let mut workers = Array.new
        let mut input_channels = Array.new
        let augmentation = DataAugmentation.default

        let mut i = 0
        loop {
            if i >= config.num_workers {
                break
            }

            let (input_sender, input_receiver) = Channel.new
            input_channels.push(input_sender)

            let worker = DataLoaderWorker.spawn(
                i,
                dataset.clone,
                input_receiver,
                output_sender.clone,
                augmentation,
                1000,
                config.seed + i
            )
            workers.push(worker)

            i = i + 1
        }

        let sampler = IndexSampler.new(dataset.size, config.shuffle, config.seed)

        ParallelDataLoader {
            @config = config,
            @dataset = dataset,
            @sampler = sampler,
            @workers = workers,
            @input_channels = input_channels,
            @output_channel = output_receiver,
            @output_sender = output_sender,
            @prefetch_queue = Array.new,
            @current_batch_idx = 0,
            @epoch = 0,
            @augmentation = augmentation,
            @stats = LoaderStats.new
        }
    }

    fn mut start_epoch {
        @epoch = @epoch + 1
        @current_batch_idx = 0
        @sampler.reset_epoch
        prefetch_batches
    }

    fn mut prefetch_batches {
        let num_to_prefetch = @config.prefetch_factor * @config.num_workers
        let num_batches = @sampler.num_batches(@config.batch_size, @config.drop_last)

        let mut i = 0
        loop {
            if i >= num_to_prefetch {
                break
            }
            let batch_idx = @current_batch_idx + i
            if batch_idx >= num_batches {
                break
            }

            let indices = @sampler.get_batch_indices(batch_idx, @config.batch_size)
            let worker_idx = batch_idx % @config.num_workers
            let message = LoaderMessage.load_batch(indices, batch_idx)
            
            @input_channels.get(worker_idx).unwrap.send(message)
            @prefetch_queue.push(batch_idx)
            
            i = i + 1
        }
    }

    fn mut next_batch -> Option[Batch] {
        let num_batches = @sampler.num_batches(@config.batch_size, @config.drop_last)
        
        if @current_batch_idx >= num_batches {
            return None
        }

        let start_time = Instant.now

        match @output_channel.receive {
            case Some(result) -> {
                if result.success {
                    @current_batch_idx = @current_batch_idx + 1
                    @stats.record_batch(result.load_time_ns)
                    
                    let new_batch_idx = @current_batch_idx + @config.prefetch_factor * @config.num_workers - 1
                    if new_batch_idx < num_batches {
                        let indices = @sampler.get_batch_indices(new_batch_idx, @config.batch_size)
                        let worker_idx = new_batch_idx % @config.num_workers
                        let message = LoaderMessage.load_batch(indices, new_batch_idx)
                        @input_channels.get(worker_idx).unwrap.send(message)
                    }
                    
                    Some(result.batch)
                } else {
                    @stats.record_error
                    None
                }
            }
            case None -> None
        }
    }

    fn has_next -> Bool {
        let num_batches = @sampler.num_batches(@config.batch_size, @config.drop_last)
        @current_batch_idx < num_batches
    }

    fn num_batches -> Int {
        @sampler.num_batches(@config.batch_size, @config.drop_last)
    }

    fn mut shutdown {
        let mut i = 0
        loop {
            if i >= @config.num_workers {
                break
            }
            @input_channels.get(i).unwrap.send(LoaderMessage.shutdown)
            i = i + 1
        }
    }

    fn get_stats -> LoaderStats {
        @stats.clone
    }
}

class LoaderStats {
    let @batches_loaded: Int
    let @total_load_time_ns: Int
    let @errors: Int
    let @avg_batch_time_ns: Int
    let @min_batch_time_ns: Int
    let @max_batch_time_ns: Int

    fn static new -> LoaderStats {
        LoaderStats {
            @batches_loaded = 0,
            @total_load_time_ns = 0,
            @errors = 0,
            @avg_batch_time_ns = 0,
            @min_batch_time_ns = Int.max_value,
            @max_batch_time_ns = 0
        }
    }

    fn mut record_batch(load_time_ns: Int) {
        @batches_loaded = @batches_loaded + 1
        @total_load_time_ns = @total_load_time_ns + load_time_ns
        @avg_batch_time_ns = @total_load_time_ns / @batches_loaded
        
        if load_time_ns < @min_batch_time_ns {
            @min_batch_time_ns = load_time_ns
        }
        if load_time_ns > @max_batch_time_ns {
            @max_batch_time_ns = load_time_ns
        }
    }

    fn mut record_error {
        @errors = @errors + 1
    }

    fn clone -> LoaderStats {
        LoaderStats {
            @batches_loaded = @batches_loaded,
            @total_load_time_ns = @total_load_time_ns,
            @errors = @errors,
            @avg_batch_time_ns = @avg_batch_time_ns,
            @min_batch_time_ns = @min_batch_time_ns,
            @max_batch_time_ns = @max_batch_time_ns
        }
    }

    fn throughput_samples_per_sec(batch_size: Int) -> Float {
        if @total_load_time_ns == 0 {
            return 0.0
        }
        let total_samples = @batches_loaded * batch_size
        let seconds = Float.from_int(@total_load_time_ns) / 1_000_000_000.0
        Float.from_int(total_samples) / seconds
    }
}

class DatasetSplit {
    let @train_indices: Array[Int]
    let @val_indices: Array[Int]
    let @test_indices: Array[Int]

    fn static random_split(size: Int, train_ratio: Float, val_ratio: Float, seed: Int) -> DatasetSplit {
        let rng = Random.new(seed)
        
        let mut indices = Array.new
        let mut i = 0
        loop {
            if i >= size {
                break
            }
            indices.push(i)
            i = i + 1
        }

        let n = indices.size
        let mut j = n - 1
        loop {
            if j <= 0 {
                break
            }
            let k = rng.int_max(j + 1)
            let temp = indices.get(j).unwrap
            indices.set(j, indices.get(k).unwrap)
            indices.set(k, temp)
            j = j - 1
        }

        let train_size = (Float.from_int(size) * train_ratio).to_int
        let val_size = (Float.from_int(size) * val_ratio).to_int

        let mut train_indices = Array.new
        let mut val_indices = Array.new
        let mut test_indices = Array.new

        i = 0
        loop {
            if i >= size {
                break
            }
            let idx = indices.get(i).unwrap
            if i < train_size {
                train_indices.push(idx)
            } else if i < train_size + val_size {
                val_indices.push(idx)
            } else {
                test_indices.push(idx)
            }
            i = i + 1
        }

        DatasetSplit {
            @train_indices = train_indices,
            @val_indices = val_indices,
            @test_indices = test_indices
        }
    }

    fn static stratified_split(labels: Array[Int], train_ratio: Float, val_ratio: Float, seed: Int) -> DatasetSplit {
        let rng = Random.new(seed)
        let size = labels.size

        let mut class_indices: Map[Int, Array[Int]] = Map.new

        let mut i = 0
        loop {
            if i >= size {
                break
            }
            let label = labels.get(i).unwrap
            match class_indices.get(label) {
                case Some(arr) -> arr.push(i)
                case None -> {
                    let arr = Array.new
                    arr.push(i)
                    class_indices.set(label, arr)
                }
            }
            i = i + 1
        }

        let mut train_indices = Array.new
        let mut val_indices = Array.new
        let mut test_indices = Array.new

        let mut iter = class_indices.iter
        loop {
            match iter.next {
                case Some(entry) -> {
                    let indices = entry.value
                    let class_size = indices.size
                    let class_train_size = (Float.from_int(class_size) * train_ratio).to_int
                    let class_val_size = (Float.from_int(class_size) * val_ratio).to_int

                    let mut j = 0
                    loop {
                        if j >= class_size {
                            break
                        }
                        let idx = indices.get(j).unwrap
                        if j < class_train_size {
                            train_indices.push(idx)
                        } else if j < class_train_size + class_val_size {
                            val_indices.push(idx)
                        } else {
                            test_indices.push(idx)
                        }
                        j = j + 1
                    }
                }
                case None -> break
            }
        }

        DatasetSplit {
            @train_indices = train_indices,
            @val_indices = val_indices,
            @test_indices = test_indices
        }
    }
}

class DistributedSampler {
    let @dataset_size: Int
    let @num_replicas: Int
    let @rank: Int
    let @shuffle: Bool
    let @seed: Int
    let @drop_last: Bool
    let @epoch: Int

    fn static new(dataset_size: Int, num_replicas: Int, rank: Int, shuffle: Bool, seed: Int) -> DistributedSampler {
        DistributedSampler {
            @dataset_size = dataset_size,
            @num_replicas = num_replicas,
            @rank = rank,
            @shuffle = shuffle,
            @seed = seed,
            @drop_last = false,
            @epoch = 0
        }
    }

    fn mut set_epoch(epoch: Int) {
        @epoch = epoch
    }

    fn get_indices -> Array[Int] {
        let rng = Random.new(@seed + @epoch)

        let mut indices = Array.new
        let mut i = 0
        loop {
            if i >= @dataset_size {
                break
            }
            indices.push(i)
            i = i + 1
        }

        if @shuffle {
            let n = indices.size
            let mut j = n - 1
            loop {
                if j <= 0 {
                    break
                }
                let k = rng.int_max(j + 1)
                let temp = indices.get(j).unwrap
                indices.set(j, indices.get(k).unwrap)
                indices.set(k, temp)
                j = j - 1
            }
        }

        let samples_per_replica = @dataset_size / @num_replicas
        let start = @rank * samples_per_replica
        let end = if @rank == @num_replicas - 1 {
            @dataset_size
        } else {
            start + samples_per_replica
        }

        let mut result = Array.new
        i = start
        loop {
            if i >= end {
                break
            }
            result.push(indices.get(i).unwrap)
            i = i + 1
        }

        result
    }
}

class CollateFunction {
    let @pad_value: Float
    let @max_length: Int
    let @dynamic_padding: Bool

    fn static default -> CollateFunction {
        CollateFunction {
            @pad_value = 0.0,
            @max_length = 512,
            @dynamic_padding = true
        }
    }

    fn collate(samples: Array[DataSample]) -> Batch {
        if @dynamic_padding {
            let mut max_len = 0
            let mut i = 0
            loop {
                if i >= samples.size {
                    break
                }
                let sample = samples.get(i).unwrap
                if sample.data.size > max_len {
                    max_len = sample.data.size
                }
                i = i + 1
            }
            max_len = min(max_len, @max_length)
            
            let mut batch = Batch.new(0, samples)
            batch.pad_to_length(max_len, @pad_value)
            batch
        } else {
            let mut batch = Batch.new(0, samples)
            batch.pad_to_length(@max_length, @pad_value)
            batch
        }
    }
}

class pub Main {
    fn pub static main {
        let mut dataset = Array.new
        let mut i = 0
        loop {
            if i >= 10000 {
                break
            }
            let mut data = Array.new
            let mut j = 0
            loop {
                if j >= 784 {
                    break
                }
                data.push(Float.from_int(j) / 784.0)
                j = j + 1
            }
            let sample = DataSample.new(i, data, i % 10)
            dataset.push(sample)
            i = i + 1
        }

        let config = DatasetConfig.default
            .with_batch_size(32)
            .with_num_workers(4)
            .with_shuffle(true)

        let mut loader = ParallelDataLoader.new(dataset, config)
        loader.start_epoch

        let mut batches_processed = 0
        loop {
            if loader.has_next == false {
                break
            }
            match loader.next_batch {
                case Some(batch) -> {
                    batches_processed = batches_processed + 1
                }
                case None -> break
            }
        }

        loader.shutdown

        let stats = loader.get_stats
    }
}
