test "constant scheduler" {
    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;
    var config = SchedulerConfig.default();
    config.scheduler_type = .constant;
    config.base_lr = 0.01;
    
    var scheduler = LearningRateScheduler.init(allocator, config);
    defer scheduler.deinit();
    
    const lr1 = scheduler.step();
    const lr2 = scheduler.step();
    const lr3 = scheduler.step();
    
    try std.testing.expectApproxEqAbs(@as(f64, 0.01), lr1, 1e-10);
    try std.testing.expectApproxEqAbs(@as(f64, 0.01), lr2, 1e-10);
    try std.testing.expectApproxEqAbs(@as(f64, 0.01), lr3, 1e-10);
}

test "step scheduler" {
    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;
    var config = SchedulerConfig.default();
    config.scheduler_type = .step;
    config.base_lr = 0.01;
    config.step_size = 10;
    config.gamma = 0.1;
    
    var scheduler = LearningRateScheduler.init(allocator, config);
    defer scheduler.deinit();
    
    for (0..9) |_| {
        _ = scheduler.step();
    }
    const lr_before = scheduler.step();
    
    const lr_after = scheduler.step();
    
    try std.testing.expect(lr_after < lr_before);
}

test "cosine annealing scheduler" {
    const allocator = std.testing.allocator;
    var config = SchedulerConfig.default();
    config.scheduler_type = .cosine_annealing;
    config.base_lr = 0.01;
    config.t_max = 100;
    config.eta_min = 0.0001;
    
    var scheduler = LearningRateScheduler.init(allocator, config);
    defer scheduler.deinit();
    
    const lr_start = scheduler.step();
    
    for (0..49) |_| {
        _ = scheduler.step();
    }
    const lr_mid = scheduler.getLr();
    
    for (0..50) |_| {
        _ = scheduler.step();
    }
    const lr_end = scheduler.getLr();
    
    try std.testing.expect(lr_start > lr_mid);
    try std.testing.expect(lr_end < lr_mid);
}

test "warmup scheduler" {
    const warmup = WarmupScheduler.init(0.01, 10, .linear);
    _ = warmup;
}

test "momentum scheduler" {
    var momentum = MomentumScheduler.init(0.85, 0.95, 100, 10, true);
    
    const m1 = momentum.step();
    try std.testing.expect(m1 >= 0.85 and m1 <= 0.95);
}

File: ./graph/graph_computation.simit
element Vertex
    position : tensor[3](float)
    velocity : tensor[3](float)
    acceleration : tensor[3](float)
    mass : float
    fixed : bool
end

element Edge
    rest_length : float
    stiffness : float
    damping : float
end

element Triangle
    area : float
    normal : tensor[3](float)
end

element Tetrahedron
    volume : float
    rest_volume : float
end

extern vertices : set{Vertex}
extern edges : set{Edge}(vertices, vertices)
extern triangles : set{Triangle}(vertices, vertices, vertices)
extern tetrahedra : set{Tetrahedron}(vertices, vertices, vertices, vertices)

func dot(a : tensor[3](float), b : tensor[3](float)) -> float
    return a(0) * b(0) + a(1) * b(1) + a(2) * b(2)
end

func cross(a : tensor[3](float), b : tensor[3](float)) -> tensor[3](float)
    var result : tensor[3](float)
    result(0) = a(1) * b(2) - a(2) * b(1)
    result(1) = a(2) * b(0) - a(0) * b(2)
    result(2) = a(0) * b(1) - a(1) * b(0)
    return result
end

func norm(v : tensor[3](float)) -> float
    return sqrt(dot(v, v))
end

func normalize(v : tensor[3](float)) -> tensor[3](float)
    var n : float = norm(v)
    if n > 1e-10
        return v / n
    end
    return v
end

func compute_edge_force(e : Edge, v0 : Vertex, v1 : Vertex) -> tensor[3](float)
    var diff : tensor[3](float) = v1.position - v0.position
    var length : float = norm(diff)
    var direction : tensor[3](float) = diff / length
    
    var stretch : float = length - e.rest_length
    var spring_force : float = e.stiffness * stretch
    
    var vel_diff : tensor[3](float) = v1.velocity - v0.velocity
    var damping_force : float = e.damping * dot(vel_diff, direction)
    
    var total_force : float = spring_force + damping_force
    
    return direction * total_force
end

proc apply_spring_forces(vertices, edges)
    for (v0, v1) in edges
        var e : Edge = edges(v0, v1)
        var force : tensor[3](float) = compute_edge_force(e, v0, v1)
        
        if not v0.fixed
            v0.acceleration += force / v0.mass
        end
        if not v1.fixed
            v1.acceleration += -force / v1.mass
        end
    end
end

proc apply_gravity(vertices)
    var gravity : tensor[3](float)
    gravity(0) = 0.0
    gravity(1) = -9.81
    gravity(2) = 0.0
    
    for v in vertices
        if not v.fixed
            v.acceleration += gravity
        end
    end
end

proc integrate_velocities(vertices, dt : float)
    for v in vertices
        if not v.fixed
            v.velocity += v.acceleration * dt
        end
    end
end

proc integrate_positions(vertices, dt : float)
    for v in vertices
        if not v.fixed
            v.position += v.velocity * dt
        end
    end
end

proc reset_accelerations(vertices)
    for v in vertices
        v.acceleration(0) = 0.0
        v.acceleration(1) = 0.0
        v.acceleration(2) = 0.0
    end
end

proc simulation_step(vertices, edges, dt : float)
    reset_accelerations(vertices)
    apply_gravity(vertices)
    apply_spring_forces(vertices, edges)
    integrate_velocities(vertices, dt)
    integrate_positions(vertices, dt)
end

func compute_triangle_area(t : Triangle, v0 : Vertex, v1 : Vertex, v2 : Vertex) -> float
    var e1 : tensor[3](float) = v1.position - v0.position
    var e2 : tensor[3](float) = v2.position - v0.position
    var cross_product : tensor[3](float) = cross(e1, e2)
    return 0.5 * norm(cross_product)
end

func compute_triangle_normal(t : Triangle, v0 : Vertex, v1 : Vertex, v2 : Vertex) -> tensor[3](float)
    var e1 : tensor[3](float) = v1.position - v0.position
    var e2 : tensor[3](float) = v2.position - v0.position
    var cross_product : tensor[3](float) = cross(e1, e2)
    return normalize(cross_product)
end

proc update_triangle_properties(vertices, triangles)
    for (v0, v1, v2) in triangles
        var t : Triangle = triangles(v0, v1, v2)
        t.area = compute_triangle_area(t, v0, v1, v2)
        t.normal = compute_triangle_normal(t, v0, v1, v2)
    end
end

func compute_tetrahedron_volume(tet : Tetrahedron, v0 : Vertex, v1 : Vertex, v2 : Vertex, v3 : Vertex) -> float
    var e1 : tensor[3](float) = v1.position - v0.position
    var e2 : tensor[3](float) = v2.position - v0.position
    var e3 : tensor[3](float) = v3.position - v0.position
    var cross_e2_e3 : tensor[3](float) = cross(e2, e3)
    return abs(dot(e1, cross_e2_e3)) / 6.0
end

proc update_tetrahedron_volumes(vertices, tetrahedra)
    for (v0, v1, v2, v3) in tetrahedra
        var tet : Tetrahedron = tetrahedra(v0, v1, v2, v3)
        tet.volume = compute_tetrahedron_volume(tet, v0, v1, v2, v3)
    end
end

func compute_volume_strain(tet : Tetrahedron) -> float
    return (tet.volume - tet.rest_volume) / tet.rest_volume
end

element NeuralVertex
    features : tensor[768](float)
    hidden : tensor[256](float)
    output : tensor[10](float)
    gradient : tensor[768](float)
end

element NeuralEdge
    weight : float
    attention : float
end

extern neural_vertices : set{NeuralVertex}
extern neural_edges : set{NeuralEdge}(neural_vertices, neural_vertices)

func relu(x : float) -> float
    if x > 0.0
        return x
    end
    return 0.0
end

func sigmoid(x : float) -> float
    return 1.0 / (1.0 + exp(-x))
end

func tanh_activation(x : float) -> float
    var exp_pos : float = exp(x)
    var exp_neg : float = exp(-x)
    return (exp_pos - exp_neg) / (exp_pos + exp_neg)
end

func gelu(x : float) -> float
    var c : float = 0.797884560803
    var x3 : float = x * x * x
    var inner : float = c * (x + 0.044715 * x3)
    return 0.5 * x * (1.0 + tanh_activation(inner))
end

proc graph_attention_layer(neural_vertices, neural_edges)
    for v in neural_vertices
        var attention_sum : tensor[256](float)
        var attention_weight_sum : float = 0.0
        
        for (src, dst) in neural_edges
            if dst == v
                var e : NeuralEdge = neural_edges(src, dst)
                var src_vertex : NeuralVertex = src
                
                for i in 256
                    attention_sum(i) += e.attention * src_vertex.hidden(i)
                end
                attention_weight_sum += e.attention
            end
        end
        
        if attention_weight_sum > 1e-10
            for i in 256
                v.hidden(i) = attention_sum(i) / attention_weight_sum
            end
        end
    end
end

proc compute_attention_weights(neural_vertices, neural_edges)
    for (src, dst) in neural_edges
        var e : NeuralEdge = neural_edges(src, dst)
        var src_vertex : NeuralVertex = src
        var dst_vertex : NeuralVertex = dst
        
        var dot_product : float = 0.0
        for i in 256
            dot_product += src_vertex.hidden(i) * dst_vertex.hidden(i)
        end
        
        e.attention = exp(dot_product / sqrt(256.0))
    end
    
    for v in neural_vertices
        var sum_exp : float = 0.0
        
        for (src, dst) in neural_edges
            if dst == v
                var e : NeuralEdge = neural_edges(src, dst)
                sum_exp += e.attention
            end
        end
        
        for (src, dst) in neural_edges
            if dst == v
                var e : NeuralEdge = neural_edges(src, dst)
                e.attention = e.attention / (sum_exp + 1e-10)
            end
        end
    end
end

proc message_passing_layer(neural_vertices, neural_edges)
    for v in neural_vertices
        var message_sum : tensor[256](float)
        var neighbor_count : int = 0
        
        for (src, dst) in neural_edges
            if dst == v
                var src_vertex : NeuralVertex = src
                var e : NeuralEdge = neural_edges(src, dst)
                
                for i in 256
                    message_sum(i) += src_vertex.hidden(i) * e.weight
                end
                neighbor_count += 1
            end
        end
        
        if neighbor_count > 0
            for i in 256
                v.hidden(i) = relu(message_sum(i) / float(neighbor_count) + v.hidden(i))
            end
        end
    end
end

proc graph_convolution(neural_vertices, neural_edges, weight_matrix : tensor[256, 256](float))
    for v in neural_vertices
        var aggregated : tensor[256](float)
        var degree : float = 0.0
        
        for (src, dst) in neural_edges
            if dst == v
                var src_vertex : NeuralVertex = src
                for i in 256
                    aggregated(i) += src_vertex.hidden(i)
                end
                degree += 1.0
            end
        end
        
        if degree > 0.0
            var inv_sqrt_degree : float = 1.0 / sqrt(degree)
            for i in 256
                aggregated(i) = aggregated(i) * inv_sqrt_degree
            end
        end
        
        var transformed : tensor[256](float)
        for i in 256
            for j in 256
                transformed(i) += weight_matrix(i, j) * aggregated(j)
            end
        end
        
        for i in 256
            v.hidden(i) = relu(transformed(i))
        end
    end
end

proc readout_layer(neural_vertices)
    for v in neural_vertices
        for i in 10
            var sum : float = 0.0
            for j in 256
                sum += v.hidden(j)
            end
            v.output(i) = sum / 256.0
        end
    end
end

func softmax_sum(neural_vertices) -> float
    var max_val : float = -1e38
    for v in neural_vertices
        for i in 10
            if v.output(i) > max_val
                max_val = v.output(i)
            end
        end
    end
    
    var sum_exp : float = 0.0
    for v in neural_vertices
        for i in 10
            sum_exp += exp(v.output(i) - max_val)
        end
    end
    
    return sum_exp
end

proc apply_softmax(neural_vertices, sum_exp : float, max_val : float)
    for v in neural_vertices
        for i in 10
            v.output(i) = exp(v.output(i) - max_val) / sum_exp
        end
    end
end

proc backward_linear(neural_vertices, grad_output : tensor[10](float), weight : tensor[768, 10](float))
    for v in neural_vertices
        for i in 768
            var grad_sum : float = 0.0
            for j in 10
                grad_sum += grad_output(j) * weight(i, j)
            end
            v.gradient(i) = grad_sum
        end
    end
end

proc aggregate_gradients(neural_vertices, neural_edges)
    for (src, dst) in neural_edges
        var e : NeuralEdge = neural_edges(src, dst)
        var dst_vertex : NeuralVertex = dst
        
        var grad_weight : float = 0.0
        for i in 256
            grad_weight += dst_vertex.gradient(i) * dst_vertex.hidden(i)
        end
        
        e.weight -= 0.001 * grad_weight
    end
end

element SparseMatrixEntry
    row : int
    col : int
    value : float
end

extern sparse_entries : set{SparseMatrixEntry}

proc sparse_matrix_vector_multiply(sparse_entries, x : tensor[1000](float), y : tensor[1000](float))
    for entry in sparse_entries
        y(entry.row) += entry.value * x(entry.col)
    end
end

proc sparse_matrix_transpose_multiply(sparse_entries, x : tensor[1000](float), y : tensor[1000](float))
    for entry in sparse_entries
        y(entry.col) += entry.value * x(entry.row)
    end
end

element MeshVertex
    position : tensor[3](float)
    normal : tensor[3](float)
    uv : tensor[2](float)
    color : tensor[4](float)
    bone_weights : tensor[4](float)
    bone_indices : tensor[4](int)
end

element MeshFace
    material_id : int
end

extern mesh_vertices : set{MeshVertex}
extern mesh_faces : set{MeshFace}(mesh_vertices, mesh_vertices, mesh_vertices)

proc compute_vertex_normals(mesh_vertices, mesh_faces)
    for v in mesh_vertices
        v.normal(0) = 0.0
        v.normal(1) = 0.0
        v.normal(2) = 0.0
    end
    
    for (v0, v1, v2) in mesh_faces
        var e1 : tensor[3](float) = v1.position - v0.position
        var e2 : tensor[3](float) = v2.position - v0.position
        var face_normal : tensor[3](float) = cross(e1, e2)
        
        v0.normal += face_normal
        v1.normal += face_normal
        v2.normal += face_normal
    end
    
    for v in mesh_vertices
        v.normal = normalize(v.normal)
    end
end

proc smooth_mesh(mesh_vertices, mesh_faces, lambda : float)
    for v in mesh_vertices
        var avg_position : tensor[3](float)
        var neighbor_count : int = 0
        
        for (v0, v1, v2) in mesh_faces
            if v0 == v or v1 == v or v2 == v
                if v0 != v
                    avg_position += v0.position
                    neighbor_count += 1
                end
                if v1 != v
                    avg_position += v1.position
                    neighbor_count += 1
                end
                if v2 != v
                    avg_position += v2.position
                    neighbor_count += 1
                end
            end
        end
        
        if neighbor_count > 0
            avg_position = avg_position / float(neighbor_count)
            v.position = v.position * (1.0 - lambda) + avg_position * lambda
        end
    end
end

element Particle
    position : tensor[3](float)
    velocity : tensor[3](float)
    force : tensor[3](float)
    density : float
    pressure : float
    mass : float
end

extern particles : set{Particle}
extern particle_neighbors : set{Edge}(particles, particles)

func kernel_poly6(r : float, h : float) -> float
    if r >= h
        return 0.0
    end
    var h2 : float = h * h
    var r2 : float = r * r
    var diff : float = h2 - r2
    var coeff : float = 315.0 / (64.0 * 3.14159265359 * pow(h, 9))
    return coeff * pow(diff, 3)
end

func kernel_spiky_gradient(r : float, h : float) -> float
    if r >= h or r < 1e-10
        return 0.0
    end
    var coeff : float = -45.0 / (3.14159265359 * pow(h, 6))
    var diff : float = h - r
    return coeff * pow(diff, 2) / r
end

proc compute_density(particles, particle_neighbors, h : float)
    for p in particles
        var density_sum : float = 0.0
        
        for (p1, p2) in particle_neighbors
            if p1 == p
                var r : tensor[3](float) = p2.position - p1.position
                var r_len : float = norm(r)
                density_sum += p2.mass * kernel_poly6(r_len, h)
            end
        end
        
        p.density = density_sum + p.mass * kernel_poly6(0.0, h)
    end
end

proc compute_pressure(particles, k : float, rho0 : float)
    for p in particles
        p.pressure = k * (p.density - rho0)
    end
end

proc compute_pressure_force(particles, particle_neighbors, h : float)
    for p in particles
        p.force(0) = 0.0
        p.force(1) = 0.0
        p.force(2) = 0.0
    end
    
    for (p1, p2) in particle_neighbors
        var r : tensor[3](float) = p2.position - p1.position
        var r_len : float = norm(r)
        
        if r_len > 1e-10 and r_len < h
            var pressure_term : float = (p1.pressure + p2.pressure) / (2.0 * p2.density)
            var grad_w : float = kernel_spiky_gradient(r_len, h)
            var direction : tensor[3](float) = r / r_len
            
            var force_magnitude : float = -p2.mass * pressure_term * grad_w
            p1.force += direction * force_magnitude
        end
    end
end

proc sph_step(particles, particle_neighbors, dt : float, h : float, k : float, rho0 : float)
    compute_density(particles, particle_neighbors, h)
    compute_pressure(particles, k, rho0)
    compute_pressure_force(particles, particle_neighbors, h)
    
    for p in particles
        p.velocity += (p.force / p.density) * dt
        p.position += p.velocity * dt
    end
end

File: ./combined_code.txt
